• Divyāvadānam

33. śārdūlakarṇāvadānam

Vai 314.001 evaṃ mayā śrutam |
Vai 314.002 ekasmin samaye bhagavāñ śrāvastyāṃ viharati sma jetavane ’nāthapiṇḍadasyārāme |
Vai 314.003 athāyuṣmānānandaḥ pūrvāhṇe nivāsya pātracīvaramādāya śrāvastīṃ mahānagarīṃ piṇḍāya prāvikṣat |
Vai 314.004 athāyuṣmānānandaḥ śrāvastīṃ piṇḍāya caritvā kṛtabhaktakṛtyo yenānyatamamudapānaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ |
Vai 314.005 tena khalu samayena tasminnudapāne prakṛtir nāma mātaṅgadārikā udakamuddharate sma |
Vai 314.006 athāyuṣmānānandaḥ prakṛtiṃ mātaṅgadārikāmetadavocat—dehi me bhagini pānīyam, pāsyāmi |
Vai 314.007 evamukte prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā āyuṣmantamānandamidamavocat—mātaṅgadārikāhamasmi bhadanta ānanda |
Vai 314.008 nāhaṃ te bhagini kulaṃ vā jātiṃ vā pṛcchāmi |
api tu sacette parityaktaṃ pānīyam, dehi, pāsyāmi |
Vai 314.009 atha prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā āyuṣmata ānandāaya pānīyamadāt |
Vai 314.010 athāyuṣmānānandaḥ pānīyaṃ pītvā prakrāntaḥ |
|
Vai 314.011 atha prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā athāyuṣmata ānandasya śarīre mukhe svare ca sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca nimittamudgṛhītvā yoniśomanasikāreṇāviṣṭā saṃrāgacittamutpādayati sma—āryo me ānandaḥ svāmī syāditi |
Vai 314.013 mātā ca me mahāvidyādharī |
sā śakṣyatyāryamānandamānayitum |
atha prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā pānīyaghaṭamādāya yena caṇḍālagṛhaṃ tenopasaṃkramya pānīyaghaṭamekānte nikṣipya svāṃ jananīmidamavocat—yatkhalu evamamba jānīyāh—ānando nāma śramaṇo mahāśramaṇagautamasya śrāvaka upasthāyakaḥ |
Vai 314.016 tamahaṃ svāminamicchāmi |
śakṣyasi tamamba ānayitum? sā tāmavocat—śaktāhaṃ putri ānandamānayituṃ sthāpayitvā yo mṛtaḥ syādyo vā vītarāgaḥ |
Vai 314.018 api ca |
rājā prasenajit kauśalaḥ śramaṇagautamamatīva sevate bhajate paryupāsane |
yadi jānīyāt, so ’yaṃ caṇḍālakulasyānarthāya pratipadyeta |
Vai 314.019 śramaṇaśca gautamo vītarāgaḥ śrūyate |
Vai 314.020 vītarāgasya mantrāh punaḥ sarvamantrānabhibhavanti |
evamuktā prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā mātaramidamavocat—sacedadamba śramaṇo gautamo vītarāgaḥ, tasyāntikācchramaṇamānandaṃ na pratilapsye, jīvitaṃ parityajeyam |
Vai 314.022 sacetpratilapsye, jīvāmi |
mā te putri jīvitaṃ parityajasi |
ānayāmi śramaṇamānandam |
|
Vai 314.024 atha prakṛtermātaṅgadārikā mātā madhye gṛhāṅganasya gomayenopalepanaṃ kṛtvā vedīmālipya darbhān saṃstīrya agniṃ pajvālya aṣṭaśatamarkapuṣpāṇāṃ gṛhītvā mantrānāvartayamānā ekaikamarkapuṣpaṃ parijapya agnau pratikṣipati sma |
Vai 314.026 tatreyaṃ vidyā bhavati—Vai 314.027 amale vimale kuṅkume sumane |
yena baddhāsi vidyut |
icchayā devo varṣati vidyotati garjati |
Vai 314.028 vismayaṃ mahārājasya samabhivardhayituṃ devebhyo manuṣyebhyo gandharvebhyaḥ śikhigrahā devā viśikhigrahā devā ānandasyāgamanāya saṃgamanāya kramaṇāya grāṇāya juhomi svāhā |
| athāyuṣmata ānandasya cittamakṣiptam |Vai 315.001

sa vihārānniṣkramya yena caṇḍālagṛhaṃ tenopasaṃkrāmati sma |
Vai 315.002 adrākṣīccaṇḍālī āyuṣmantamānandaṃ dūrādevāgacchantam |
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ prakṛtiṃ duhitaramidamavocat—ayamasau putri śramaṇa ānanda āgacchati |
Vai 315.003 śayanaṃ prajñapaya |
Vai 315.004 atha prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā hṛṣṭatuṣṭā pramuditamanā āyuṣmata ānandasya śayyāṃ prajñapayati sma |
|
Vai 315.005 athāyuṣmānāndo yena caṇḍālagṛhaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ |
upasaṃkramya vedīmupaniśrityāsthāt |
ekāntasthitaḥ sa punarāyuṣmānāndaḥ prārodīt |
Vai 315.006 aśrūṇi pravartayamāna evamāha—vyasanaprāpto ’hamasmi |
Vai 315.007 na ca me bhagavān samanvāharati |
atha bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandaṃ samanvāharati sma |
Vai 315.008 samanvāhṛtya saṃbuddhamantraiścaṇḍālamantrān pratihanti sma |
tatreyaṃ vidyā—Vai 315.009 sthitiracyutiḥ sunītiḥ |
svasti sarvaprāṇibhyaḥ |
|
Vai 315.010 saraḥ prasannaṃ nirdeṣaṃ praśāntaṃ sarvato ’bhayam |
Vai 315.011 ītayo yatra śāmyanti bhayāni calitāni ca (1)|
Vai 315.012 tadvai devā namasyanti sarvasiddhāśca yoginaḥ |
Vai 315.013 etena satyavākyena svastyānandāsya bhikṣave (2)|
Vai 315.014 athāyuṣmānāndaḥ pratihatacaṇḍālamantraścaṇḍālagṛhānniṣkramya yena svako vihārastenopasaṃkramitumārabdhaḥ |
|
Vai 315.016 adrākṣītprakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā ānandamāyuṣmantaṃ pratigacchantam |
dṛṣṭvā ca punaḥ svāṃ jananīmidamavocat—ayamasau mātaḥ śramaṇa ānandaḥ pratigacchati |
Vai 315.017 tāmāha mātā—niyataṃ putri śramaṇena gautamena samanvāhṛto bhaviṣyati |
Vai 315.018 tena mama mantrāḥ pratihatā bhaviṣyanti |
prakṛtirāha—kiṃ punaramba balavattarāḥ śramaṇasya gautamasya mantrā nāsmākam? tāmāha mātā—balavattarāḥ śramaṇasya gautamasya mantrā nāsmākam |
Vai 315.020 ye putri mantrāḥ sarvalokasya prabhavanti, tān mantrāñ śramaṇo gautama ākāṅkṣamāṇaḥ pratihanti |
Vai 315.021 na punarlokaḥ prabhavati śramaṇasya gautamasya mantrān pratihantum |
Vai 315.022 evaṃ balavattarāḥ śramaṇasya gautamasya mantrāḥ |
|
Vai 315.023 athāyuṣmānānando yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntaḥ |
upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt |
Vai 315.024 ekāntasthitamāyuṣmantamānandaṃ bhagavānidamavocat—udgṛhṇa rvamānanda imāṃ ṣaḍakṣarīvidyām |
Vai 315.025 dhāraya vācaya paryavāpnuhi ātmano hitāya sukhāya bhikṣūṇāṃ bhikṣuṇīnāmupāsakānāmupāsikānāṃ hitāya sukhāya |
Vai 315.026 iyamānanda ṣaḍakṣarīvidyā ṣaḍbhiḥ samyaksambuddhairbhāṣitā, caturbhiśca mahārājaiḥ, śakreṇa devānāmindreṇa, brahmaṇā ca sahāpatinā |
Vai 315.027 mayā caitarhi śākyamuninā samyaksambuddhena bhāṣitā |
Vai 315.028 tvamapyetarhi ānanda tāṃ dhārasya vācaya paryavāpnuhi |
Vai 315.029 yaduta tadyathā—Vai 315.030 aṇḍare pāṇḍare kāraṇḍe keyūre ’rcihaste kharagrīve bandhumati vīramati dhara vidha cilimile vilo:aya viṣāṇi loke |
Vai 315.031 viṣa cala cala |
golamati gaṇḍavile cilimile sātiniṃne yathāsaṃvibhakte golamati gaṇḍavilāyai svāhā |
|
yaḥ kaścidānanda ṣaḍakṣaryā vidyayā paritrāṇaṃ svastyayanaṃ kuryāt, sa yadi vadhārho bhavet, daṇḍena mucyate, daṇḍārhaḥ prahāreṇa, prahārārhaḥ, paribhāṣaṇayā, paribhāṣaṇārho romaharṣaṇena, romaharṣaṇārhaḥ punareva mucyate |
Vai 316.003 nāhamānanda taṃ samanupaśyāmi sadevaloke samāraloke sabrahmaloke saśramaṇabrāhmaṇikāyāṃ prajāyāṃ sadevamānuṣikāyāṃ sāsurāyām yastvanayā ṣaḍkṣaryā vidyayā rakṣāyāṃ kṛtāyāṃ rakṣāsūtre bāhau baddhe svastyayane kṛte abhibhavituṃ śaknoti varjayitvā paurāṇaṃ karmavipākam |
|
Vai 316.007 atha prakṛtirmāraṅgadārikā tasyā eva rātryā atyayāt śiraḥsnātā anāhatadūṣyaprāvṛtā muktāmālyābharaṇā yena śrāvastī nagarī tenopasaṃkramya nagaradvāre kapāṭamūle niśrityāsthādāyuṣmantamānandamāgamayamānā—niyatamanena mārgeṇa ānando ānando bhikṣurāgamiṣyatīti |
Vai 316.009 dadarśāyuṣmānānandaḥ prakṛtiṃ mātaṅgadārikāṃ pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhām |
Vai 316.010 dṛṣṭvā ca punarjehrīyamāṇarūpo ’pragalbhāyamānarūpo duḥkhī durmanāḥ śīghraṃ śīghraṃ śrāvastyā vinirgamya yena jetavanaṃ tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ |
Vai 316.012 upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvaikānte ’sthāt |
ekāntasthita āyucmānānando bhagavantamidamavocat—iyaṃ me bhagavan prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā pṛṣṭhataḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ samanubaddhā gacchantamanu gacchati, tiṣṭhantamanu tiṣṭhati |
Vai 316.014 yadyadeva kulaṃ pinṇḍāya praviśāmi, tasya tasyaiva dvāre tūṣṇībhūtā tiṣṭhati |
Vai 316.015 trāhi me bhagavan, trāhi me sugata |
evamukte bhagavānāyuṣmantamānandamidamavocat—kiṃ te prakṛte mātaṅgadārike ānandena bhikṣuṇā? prakṛtirāha—svāminaṃ bhadanta ānandamicchāmi |
Vai 316.017 bhagavānāha—anujñātāsi prakṛte mātāpitṛbhyāmānandāya? anujñātāsmi bhagavan, anujñātāsmi sugata |
Vai 316.018 bhagavānāha—tena hi saṃmukhaṃ mamānujñāpaya tvam |
Vai 316.019 atha prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā bhagavataḥ pratiśrutya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavato ’ntikāt prakrāntā |
Vai 316.020 yena svakau mātāpitarau tenopasaṃkrāntā |
Vai 316.021 upasaṃkramya mātāpitroḥ pādāñ śirasā vanditvā ekānte ’sthāt |
ekāntasthitā svakau mātāpitarāvidamavocat—saṃmukhaṃ me amba tāta śramaṇasya gautamasya ānandāya utsṛjatam |
Vai 316.023 atha prakṛtermātaṅgadārikāyā mātāpitarau prakṛtimādāyā yena bhagavāṃstenopasaṃkrāntau |
Vai 316.024 upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte ’sthāt |
Vai 316.025 ekāntasthitā bhagavantametadavocat—imau tau bhagavan mātāpitarāvāgatau |
Vai 316.026 atha bhagavān prakṛtermātaṅgadārikāyā mātāpitarāvidamavocat—anujñātā yuvābhyāṃ prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā ānandāyeti? tāvāhatuh—anujñātā bhagavan, anujñātā sugata |
Vai 316.028 tena hi yūyaṃ prakṛtimapahāya gacchata svagṛham |
atha prakṛtermātaṅgadārikāyā mātāpitarau bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā bhagavantaṃ triḥ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya bhagavato ’ntikātprakrāntau |
|
Vai 316.031 atha prakṛtermātaṅgadārikāyā mātāpitarāvaciraprakrāntau viditvā bhagavān prakṛtiṃ mātaṅgadārikāmidamavocat—arthikāsi prakṛte ānandena bhikṣūṇā? prakṛtirāha—arthikāsmi bhagavan, Vai 317.000arthikāsmi sugata |
Vai 317.001 tena hi prakṛte ya ānandasya veṣaḥ, sa tvayā dhārayitavyaḥ |
sā āha—dhārayāmi bhagavan, dhārayāmi sugata |
Vai 317.002 pravrajayatu māṃ sugata, pravrajayatu māṃ bhagavān |
atha bhagavān prakṛtiṃ mātaṅgadārikāmidamavocat—ehi tvaṃ bhikṣuṇī, cara brahmacaryam |
Vai 317.003 evamukte prakṛtirmātaṅgadārikā bhagavatā muṇḍā kāṣāyapravṛtā |
Vai 317.004 atha bhagavān prakṛtiṃ mātaṅgadārikāmehibhikṣuṇīvādena pravrājayitvā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśayati sma, samādāpayati sma, smuttejayati sma, saṃpraharṣayati sma |
Vai 317.006 yeyaṃ kathā dīrgharātraṃ saṃsārasamāpannānāṃ pratikūlā śravaṇīyā, tadyathā—dānakathā śīlakathā svargakathā kāmeṣvādīnavaṃ niḥsaraṇaṃ bhayaṃ saṃkleśavyavadānam, bodhipakṣāṃstān dharmān bhagavān prakṛtyai bhikṣuṇyai saṃprakāśayati sma |
Vai 317.008 atha prakṛtirbhikṣuṇī bhagavatā dharmyayā kathayā saṃdarśitā samādāpitā samuttejitā saṃpraharṣitā hṛṣṭacittā kalyāṇacittāa muditacittā vinīvaraṇacittā ṛjucittākhilacittā bhavyā dharmadeśitamājñātum |
Vai 317.010 yadā ca bhagavāñ jñātaḥ prakṛtiṃ bhikṣuṇīṃ hṛṣṭacittāṃ kalyāṇacittāṃ muditacittāṃ vinīvaraṇacittāṃ bhavyāṃ pratibalāṃ sāmutkarṣikīṃ dharmadeśanāmājñātum, tadā yeyaṃ bhagavatāṃ buddhānāṃ caturāyasatyaprativedhikī dhrmadeśanā, yaduta duḥkhaṃ samudayo nirodho mārgaḥ, tāṃ bhagavān prakṛterbhikṣuṇyā vistareṇa saṃprakāśayati sma |
Vai 317.014 atha prakṛtirbhikṣuṇī tasminnevāsane niṣaṇṇā caturāyasatyānyabhijñātāsīt, duḥkhaṃ samudayaṃ nirodhaṃ mārgam |
Vai 317.015 tadyathā vastramapagatakālakaṃ rajanopagataṃ raṅgodake prakṣiptaṃ samyageva raṅgaṃ pratigṛhṇīyāt, evameva prakṛtirbhikṣuṇī tasminnevāsane niṣaṇṇā caturāyasatyāni abhisamayati sma, tadyathā—duḥkhaṃ samudayaṃ nirodhaṃ mārgam |
|
Vai 317.018 atha praṛtirbhikṣuṇī dṛṣṭadharmā prāptadharmā viditadharmā akopyadharmā paryavasitadharmā adhigatārthalābhasaṃvṛttā tīrṇakāṅkṣāvicikitsā vigatakathaṃkathā vaiśāradyaprāptā aparapratyayā ananyaneyā śāstuḥ śāsane anudharmacāriṇī ājāneyamānā dharmeṣu bhagavataḥ pādayoḥ śirasā nipatya bhagavantamidamavocat—atyayo me bhagvan, atyayo me sugata |
Vai 317.021 yathā bālā yathā mūḍhā yathā avyaktā yathā akuśalā duṣṭrajñajātīyā, yāhamānandaṃ bhikṣuṃ svāmivādena samudācārṣam |
Vai 317.023 sāhaṃ bhadanta atyayamatyayataḥ paśyāmi |
atyayamatyayato dṛṣṭvā deśayāmi |
atyayamatyayata āviṣkaromi |
Vai 317.024 āyatyāṃ saṃvaramāpadye |
atastasyā mama bhagavann atyayamatyayato jānātu pratigṛhṇātu anukampāmupādāya |
Vai 317.025 bhagavānāha—āyatyāṃ saṃvarāya sthitvā tvaṃ prakṛte atyayamatyayato ’dhyāgamaḥ |
Vai 317.026 yathā bālā yathā mūḍhā yathā avyaktā yathā akuśalā duṣprajñajātīyā tvamānandaṃ bhikṣuṃ svāmivādena samudācarasīti |
Vai 317.027 yataśca tvaṃ prakṛte atyayaṃ jānāsi, atyayaṃ paśyasi, āyatyāṃ ca saṃvaramāpadyase, ahamapi te ’tyayamatyayato gṛhṇāmi |
Vai 317.028 vṛddhireva te prakṛte pratikāṅkṣitavyā kuśalānāṃ dharmāṇām, na hāniḥ |
Vai 317.029 atha prakṛtirbhikṣuṇī bhagavatābhinanditānuśiṣṭā ekā vyapakṛṣṭā apramattā ātāpinī smṛtimatī saṃprajānā prahitāni viviktāni viharati sma |
Vai 317.031 yadarthaṃ kuladuhitaraḥ keśānavatārya kāṣāyāṇi vastrāṇyācchādya samyageva śraddhayā agārādanāgārikāṃ pravrajanti, tadanuttarabrahmacaryaparyavasānaṃ dṛṣṭa eva dharme svayamabhijñāya sākṣākṛtyopasampadyaVai 318.000 pravedayate sma—kṣīṇā me jātiḥ, uṣitaṃ brahmacaryam, kṛtaṃ karaṇīyam, nāparamasmādbhavaṃ prajānāmīti |
|
Vai 318.002 aśrauṣuḥ śrāvasteyakā brāhmaṇagṛhapatayah—bhagavatā kila caṇḍāladārikā pravrājiteti |
Vai 318.004 śrutvā ca punaravadhyāyanti—kathaṃ hi nāma caṇḍāladārikā bhikṣūṇāṃ samyakcaryāṃ cariṣyati? bhikṣuṇīnāmupāsakānāmupāsikānāṃ samyakcaryāṃ cariṣyati? kathaṃ hi nāma caṇḍāladārikā brahmakṣatriyagṛhapatimahāśālakuleṣu pravekṣyati?Vai 318.007 aśrauṣīdrājā prasenajitkauśalah—bhagavatā caṇḍāladārikā pravrajiteti |
Vai 318.008 śrutvā ca punaravadhyāyati—kathaṃ hi nāma caṇḍāladārikā bhikṣūṇāṃ samyakcaryāṃ cariṣyati? bhikṣuṇīnāmupāsakānāmupādikānāṃ samyakcaryāṃ cariṣyati? kathaṃ brāhmaṇakṣatriyagṛhapatimahāśālakuleṣu pravekṣyati? vimṛśya ca bhadram yānam yojayitvā bhadram yānamabhiruhya saṃbahulaiśca śrāvasteyairbrāhmaṇagṛhapatibhiḥ parivṛtaḥ puraskṛtaḥ śrāvastyā niryāti sma |
Vai 318.011 yena jetavanamanāthapiṇḍadasyārāmaḥ, tenopasaṃkrāntaḥ |
Vai 318.012 tasya khalu yāvatī yānasya bhūmiḥ, tāvadyānena gatvāṃ sa yānādavatīrya pattikāyaparivṛtaḥ pattikāyapuraskṛtaḥ padbhyāmevārāmaṃ pravikṣat |
Vai 318.013 praviśya yena bhagavāṃstenopasṃkrāntaḥ |
Vai 318.014 upasaṃkramya bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇaḥ |
te ’pi saṃbahulāḥ śrāvasteyakā brāhmaṇakṣatriyagṛhapatayo bhagavataḥ pādau śirasā vanditvā ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ |
Vai 318.016 apyaikatyā bhagavatā sārdhaṃ saṃmukhaṃ saṃrañjanīṃ saṃmodinīṃ vividhāṃ kathāṃ vyatisārya ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ |
Vai 318.017 apyaikatyā bhagavataḥ purataḥ svakasvakāni mātāpaitṛkāṇi nāmagotrāṇi nāmagotrāṇi anuśrāvya ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ |
Vai 318.018 apyaikatyā yena bhagavāṃstenāñjaliṃ praṇamya ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ |
Vai 318.019 apyaikatyāstūṣṇīmbhūtā ekānte niṣaṇṇāḥ |
|
Vai 318.020 atha bhagavān rājānaṃ prasenajitaṃ kauśalamārabhya teṣāṃ ca saṃbahulānāṃ śrāvasteyakānāṃ brāhmaṇakṣatriyagṛhapatīnāṃ cetasā cittamājñāya prakṛterbhikṣuṇyāḥ pūrvanivāsamārabhya bhikṣūnāmantrayate sma—icchatha yūyaṃ bhikṣavastathāgatasya saṃmukhaṃ prakṛterbhikṣuṇyāḥ pūrvanivāsamārabhya dharmakathāṃ śrotum? bhikṣavo bhagavantamāhuh—etasya bhagavan kālaḥ, etasya sugata samayaḥ, yadbhagavān prakṛterbhikṣuṇyāḥ pūrvanivāsamārabhya dharmakathāṃ kathayet, yadbhagavataḥ śrutvā bhikṣavo dhārayiṣyanti |
Vai 318.025 bhagavānāha—tena hi bhikṣavaḥ śṛṇuta, sādhu ca suṣṭhu ca manasikuruta, bhāṣiṣye |
evaṃ sādhu bhagavanniti te bhikṣavo bhagavataḥ pratyaśrauṣuḥ |
Vai 318.026 bhagavāṃstānidamavocat—Vai 318.027 bhūtapūrvaṃ bhikṣavo ’tīte ’dhvani gaṅgātaṭe atimuktakadalīpāṭalakāmalakīvanagahanapradeśe tatra triśaṅkur nāma mātaṅgarājāḥ prativasati sma saṃbahulaiśca mātaṅgasahasraiḥ sārdham |
Vai 318.028 sa punaribhikṣavastriśaṅkurmātaṅgarājaḥ pūrvajanmādhītān vedān smanusmarati sma sāṅgopāṅgān sarahasyān sanighaṇṭakaiṭabhān sākṣaraprabhedānitihāsapañcamān, anyāni ca śāstrāṇi padakośo? vaiyākaraṇo lokāyate yajñamantre mahāpuruṣalakṣaṇe niṣṇāto niṣkāṅkṣaḥ |
Vai 318.031 bhāṣyaṃ ca yathādharmaṃ vedavratapadānyanuśrutaṃ ca bhāṣate sma |
Vai 318.032 tasya triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasya śārdūlakarṇo nāma kumāro ’bhūdutpannaḥ |
Vai 319.000rūpataśca kulataśca śīlataśca guṇataśca sarvaguṇaiścopeto ’bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ paramayā śubhavarṇapuṣkalatayā samanvāgataḥ |
Vai 319.002 atha triśaṅkurmātaṅgarājaḥ śārdūlakarṇaṃ kumāraṃ pūrvajanmādhītān vedānadhyāpayati sma yaduta sāṅgopāṅgān sarahasyān sanighaṇṭakaiṭabhān sākṣaraprabhedānitihāsapañcamānm, anyāni ca śāstrāṇi, bhāṣyaṃ ca yathādharmaṃ vedavratapadāni |
|
Vai 319.005 atha triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasyaitadabhavat—ayaṃ mama putraḥ śārdūlakarṇo nāma kumārah upeto rūpataśca kulataśca śīlataśca guṇataśca, sarvaguṇopetp^bhirūpo darśanīyaḥ prāsādikaḥ, paramayā ca varṇapuṣkalatayā samanvāgataḥ |
Vai 319.007 cīrṇavrato ’dhītamantro vedapāragaḥ |
samayo ’yam yannvahamasya niveśanadharmaṃ kariṣye |
Vai 319.008 tatkuto nvahaṃ śārdūlakarṇasya putrasya śīlavatīṃ guṇavatīṃ rūpavatīṃ pratirūpāṃ prajāvatīṃ labheyamiti?Vai 319.010 tasmin khalu samaye puṣkarasārī nāma brāhmaṇa utkūṭaṃ nāma droṇamukhaṃ paribhuṅkte sma sasaptotsadaṃ stṛṇakāṣṭhodakaṃ dhānyasahagataṃ rājñāgnidattena brahmadeyaṃ dattam |
Vai 319.011 puṣkarasārī punarbrāhmaṇa upeto mātṛtaḥ pitṛtaḥ saṃśuddho gṛhiṇyāmanā kule jātyāṃ vā kṣipto jātivādena gotravādena yāvadāsaptamamātāmahapitāmaham |
Vai 319.013 yugapadupādhyāyo ’dhyāpako mantradharastrayāṇāṃ vedānāṃ pāragaḥ sāṅgopāṅgānāṃ sarahasyānāṃ sanighaṇṭakeiṭabhānāṃ sākṣaraprabhedānāmitihāsapañcamānāṃ padakośo vaiyākaraṇaḥ |
Vai 319.015 lokāyatayajñamantramahāpuruṣalakṣaṇeṣu pāragaḥ |
sphītamutkūṭaṃ nāma droṇamukhaṃ paribhuṅkte |
Vai 319.016 puṣkarasāriṇo brāhmaṇasya prakṛtir nāma māṇavikā duhitā bhūtā |
upetā rūpataśca kulataśca śīlataśca guṇataśca, sarvaguṇopetā abhirūpā darśanīyā prāsādikā paramayā varṇapuṣkalatayā samanvāgatā śīlavatī guṇavatī |
|
Vai 319.019 atha triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasyaitadabhavat—astyuttarapūrveṇotkūṭo nāma droṇamukhaḥ |
tatra puṣkarasāro nāma brāhmaṇaḥ prativasati |
Vai 319.020 upeto mātṛtaḥ pitṛto yāvat traivedike pravacane vistareṇa |
Vai 319.021 sa cotkūṭaṃ droṇamukhaṃ paribhuṅkte sasaptotsadaṃ satṛṇakāṣṭhodakaṃ dhānyabhogaiḥ sahagataṃ rājñāgnidattena brahmadeyaṃ dattam |
Vai 319.022 tasya puṣkarasāriṇo brāhmaṇasya prakṛtir nāma māṇavikā duhitā upetā rūpataśca kulataśca śīlataśca srvaguṇopetā abhirūpā darśanīyā prāsādikā paramayā varṇapuṣkalatayā samanvāgatā śīlavatī guṇavatī putrasya me śārdūlakarṇasya pratirūpā patnī bhaviṣyatīti |
Vai 319.025 atha triśaṅkurmātaṅgarāja etamevārthaṃ bahulaṃ rātrau cintayitvā vitarkya tasyā eva rātryā atyayāt pratyūṣakālasamaye srvaśvetaṃ vaḍavārathamabhiruhya mahatā śvapākagaṇena amātyagaṇena parivṛtaścaṇḍālanagarānniṣkramyottareṇa prāgacchadyenotkūṭaṃ droṇamukham |
Vai 319.027 atha triśaṅkurmātaṅgarāja utkūṭasyottarapūrveṇa sumanaskaṃ nāmodyānaṃ nānāvṛkṣasaṃchannaṃ nānāvṛkṣakusumitaṃ nānādvijanikūjitaṃ nandanamiva devānāṃ tadupasaṃkrāntaḥ |
Vai 319.029 upasaṃkramya brāhmaṇaṃ puṣkarasāriṇamāgamayamāno ’sthāt—brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī māṇavakān mantrān vācayitumihāgamiṣyatīti |
|
Vai 319.031 atha brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī tasyā rva rātryā atyayāt srvaśvetaṃ vaḍavārathamabhiruhya śiṣyagaṇaparivṛtaḥ pañcamatrairmāṇavakaśataiḥ puraskṛta utkūṭānniryāti sma brāhmaṇān mantrān Vai 320.000vācayitum |
Vai 320.001 adrākṣīttriśaṅkurmātaṅgarājo brāhmaṇaṃ puṣkarasāriṇaṃ sūryamivodayantaṃ tejasā, jvalantamiva hutavaham, yajñamiva brāhmaṇaparivṛtam, śakramiva devagaṇaparivṛtam, haimavantamivauṣadhibhiḥ, samudramiva ratnaiḥ, candramiva nakṣatraiḥ, vaiśravaṇamiva yakṣagaṇaiḥ, brahmāṇamiva devarṣigaṇaiḥ parivṛtaṃ śobhamānam |
Vai 320.004 dūrata evāgacchantaṃ dṛṣṭvā ca enaṃ pratyudgamya yathādharmaṃ kṛtvedamavocat—haṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin, svāgatam, āyāhi |
Vai 320.005 kāryaṃ ca te vakṣyāmi, tacchrūyatām |
Vai 320.006 evamukte brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī triśaṅkuṃ mātaṅgarājamidamavocat—na hi bhostriśaṅko śakyaṃ brāhmaṇena saha bhoḥkāraṃ kartum |
Vai 320.007 ahaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasāriñ śaknomi bhoḥkāraṃ kartum |
yacchakyaṃ me kartuṃ bhavati, naiva tacchakyaṃ te kartum |
Vai 320.008 api tu catvāro bhoḥ puṣkarasārin puruṣasya kāryamānambhāḥ pūrvasamārabdhā bhavanti yaduta ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā ātmīyārthaṃ vā sarvabhūtasaṃgrahārthaṃ vā |
Vai 320.010 idaṃ cātra mahattaraṃ kāryam |
yatte vyākhyāsyāmi, tacchrūyatāam |
putrāya me śārdūlakarṇāya prakṛtiṃ duhitaramutsṛja bhāryārthāya |
Vai 320.011 yāvantaṃ kulaśulkaṃ manyase, tāvantaṃ dāsyāmi |
|
Vai 320.013 idaṃ ca khalu punarvacanaṃ śrutvā triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasya bhṛśaṃ brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī abhiṣiktaḥ kupitaścaṇḍībhūto ’nāttamanāḥ kopaṃ ca dveṣaṃ ca mrakṣaṃ ca tatpratyayātsaṃjanitvā lalāṭe triśikhāṃ bhṛkuṭīṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhaṃ dhamayitvā akṣiṇī parivartya nakulapiṅgalāṃ dṛṣṭimutpādya triśaṅkuṃ mātaṅgarājamidamavocat—dhig grāmyaviṣaya caṇḍāla, nedaṃ śvapākavacanam yuktam, yastvaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragaṃ hīnaścaṇḍālayonijo bhūtvā icchasyavamarditum |
Vai 320.017 bho durmate—Vai 320.018 prakṛtiṃ tvaṃ na jānāsi ātmānaṃ cābhimanyase |
Vai 320.019 bālāgre sarṣapaṃ mā bhoḥ sthāpaya mā kleśamāgamaḥ |
Vai 320.020 mā prārthayāprārthanīyāṃ vāyuṃ pāśena bandhaya (3)|
Vai 320.021 na hi cāmīkaraṃ mūḍha bhavedbhasma kadācana |
Vai 320.022 prakāśe vāndhakāre kiṃ viśeṣo nopalabhyate (4)|
Vai 320.023 caṇḍālayonijastvaṃ hi dvijātiḥ punarapyaham |
Vai 320.024 hīnaḥ śreṣṭhena saṃbandhaṃ mūḍha prārthayase katham (5)|
Vai 320.025 caṇḍālayonibhūtastvamahamasmi dvijātijaḥ |
Vai 320.026 na hi śreṣṭhaḥ prahīnena saṃbandhaṃ kartumicchati |
Vai 320.027 śreṣṭhāḥ śreṣṭhairhi saṃbandhaṃ kurvantīha dvijātayaḥ (6)|
Vai 320.028 vidyayā ye tu saṃpannāḥ saṃśuddhāścaraṇena ca |
Vai 320.029 jātyā caivānabhikṣiptā mantraiḥ paramatāṃ gatāḥ (7)|
Vai 320.030 adhyāpakā mantradharāstriṣu vedeṣu pāragāḥ |
Vai 320.031 nighaṇṭakaiṭabhān vedān brāhmaṇā ye hyadhīyate |
Vai 320.032 taistādṛṣairhi saṃbandhaṃ kurvantīha dvijātayaḥ (8)|
na hi śreṣṭho hi hīnena saṃbandhaṃ kartumicchati |
Vai 321.002 prārthayase ’prārthanīyāṃ vāyuṃ pāśena bandhitum |
Vai 321.003 yadasmābhiśca saṃbandhamiha tvaṃ kartumicchasi (9)|
Vai 321.004 jugupsitaḥ sarvaloke kṛpaṇaḥ puruṣādhamaḥ |
Vai 321.005 gaccha tvaṃ vṛṣala kṣipraṃ kimasmānavamanyase (10)|
Vai 321.006 caṇḍālāḥ saha caṇḍālaiḥ pukkasāḥ saha pukkasaiḥ |
Vai 321.007 kurvantīhaiva saṃbandhaṃ jātibhirjātireva ca (11)|
Vai 321.008 brāhmaṇā brāhmaṇaiḥ sārdhaṃ kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyaiḥ saha |
Vai 321.009 sārdhaṃ vaiśyāstathā vaiśyaiḥ śūdrāḥ śūdraistathā saha (12)|
Vai 321.010 sadṛśāḥ sadṛśaiḥ sārdhamāvahanti parasparam |
Vai 321.011 na hi kurvanti caṇḍālāḥ saṃbandhaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ saha (13)|
Vai 321.012 sarvajātivihīno ’si sarvavarṇajugupsitaḥ |
Vai 321.013 kathaṃ hīnaśca śreṣṭhena saṃbandhaṃ kartumicchasi (14)|
Vai 321.014 idaṃ punarvacanaṃ śrutvā brāhmaṇasya puṣkarasāriṇas triśaṅkurmātaṅgarāja idamavocat—Vai 321.015 yathā bhasmani sauvarṇe viśeṣa upalabhyate |
Vai 321.016 brāhmaṇe vānyajātau vā na viśeṣo ’sti vai tathā (15)|
Vai 321.017 yathā prakāśatamasorviśeṣa upalabhyate |
Vai 321.018 brāhmaṇe vānyajātau vā na viśeṣo ’sti vai tathā (16)|
Vai 321.019 na hi brāhmaṇa ākāśānmaruto vā samutthitaḥ |
Vai 321.020 bhittvā vā pṛthivīṃ jāto jātavedā yathāraṇeḥ (17)|
Vai 321.021 brāhmaṇā yonito jātāścaṇḍālā api yonitaḥ |
Vai 321.022 śreṣṭhatve vṛṣalatve ca kiṃ vā paśyasi kāraṇam (18)|
Vai 321.023 brāhmaṇe ’pi mṛtotsṛṣṭo jugupsyo ’śucirucyate |
Vai 321.024 varṇāstathaiva cāpyanye kā nu tatra viśeṣatā (19)|
Vai 321.025 yatkiṃcitpāpakaṃ karma kilbiṣaṃ kalireva ca |
Vai 321.026 sattvānāmupaghātāya brāhmaṇaistatprakāśitam (20)|
Vai 321.027 iti karmāṇi caitāni prakāśitāni brāhmaṇaiḥ |
Vai 321.028 karmabhirdāruṇaiścāpi "puṇyo ’ham" bruvate dvijāḥ (21)|
Vai 321.029 māṃsaṃ khāditukāmaistu brāhmaṇairupakalpitam |
Vai 321.030 mantrairhi prokṣitāḥ santaḥ svargaṃ gacchantyajaiḍakāḥ (22)|
yadeṣa mārgaḥ svagārya kasmānna brāhmaṇā hyamī |
Vai 322.002 ātmānamathavā bandhūnmantraiḥ saṃprokṣayanti vai (23)|
Vai 322.003 mātaraṃ pitaraṃ caiva bhrātaraṃ bhaginīṃ tathā |
Vai 322.004 putra duhitaraṃ bhāryāṃ dvijā na prokṣayantyamī (24)|
Vai 322.005 mitraṃ jñātiṃ sakhīṃ vāpi ye vā viṣayavāsinaḥ |
Vai 322.006 prokṣitāste ’pi vā mantraiḥ sarve yāsyanti sadgatim (25)|
Vai 322.007 sarve yajñaiḥ samāhūtā gamiṣyanti satāṃ gatim |
Vai 322.008 paśubhiḥ kiṃ nu bho yaṣṭairātmānaṃ kiṃ na yakṣyase (26)|
Vai 322.009 na prokṣaṇair na mantraiśca svargaṃ gacchantyajaiṭakāḥ |
Vai 322.010 na hyeṣa mārgaḥ svargāya mithyāprokṣaṇamucyate (27)|
Vai 322.011 brāhmaṇai raudracittaistu paryāyo hyeṣa cintitaḥ |
Vai 322.012 māṃsaṃ khāditukāmaistu prokṣaṇaṃ kalpitaṃ paśoḥ (28)|
Vai 322.013 anyaccāhaṃ pravakṣyāmi brāhmaṇairyat prakalpitam |
Vai 322.014 pātakā hi samākhyātā brāhmaṇeṣu caturvidhāḥ (29)|
Vai 322.015 suvarṇacauryaṃ madyaṃ gurudārābhimardanam |
Vai 322.016 brahmaghnatā ca catvāraḥ pātakā brāhmaṇeṣvamī (30)|
Vai 322.017 suvarṇaharaṇaṃ varjyaṃ steyamanyanna vidyate |
Vai 322.018 suvarṇam yo haredvipraḥ sa tenā^brāhmaṇo bhavet (31)|
Vai 322.019 surāpānaṃ na pātavyamannapānam yatheṣṭataḥ |
Vai 322.020 surāṃ tu yaḥ pibedvipraḥ sa tenābrāhmaṇo bhavet (32)|
Vai 322.021 gurudārā na gantavyā anyadārā yatheṣṭataḥ |
Vai 322.022 gurudārāṃ tu yo gacchetsa tenābrāhmaṇo bhavet (33)|
Vai 322.023 na hanyād brāhmaṇaṃ hyakaṃ hanyādanyānanekaśaḥ |
Vai 322.024 hanyāttu brāhmaṇam yo vai sa tenābrāhmaṇo bhavet (34)|
Vai 322.025 ityete pātakā hyuktā brāhmaṇeṣu caturvidhāḥ |
Vai 322.026 bhavatyabrāhmaṇā yena tato ’nye ’pātakāḥ smṛtāḥ (35)|
Vai 322.027 kṛtvā caturṇāmekaikaṃ bhavedabrāhmaṇastu saḥ |
Vai 322.028 labhate na ca sāmīcīṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ samāgame |
Vai 322.029 āsanaṃ codakaṃ caiva vyutthānaṃ sa na cārhati (36)|
Vai 322.030 tasy niḥsaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇaiḥ patitasya tu |
Vai 322.031 vrataṃ vai sa samādāya punarbrāhmaṇatāṃ vrajet (37)|
asau dvādaśavarṣāṇi dhārayitvā kharājinam |
Vai 323.002 khaṭvāṅgamucchritaṃ kṛtvā mṛtaśīrṣe ca bhijanam (38)|
Vai 323.003 etadvrataṃ samādāya niścayena nirantaram |
Vai 323.004 pūrṇe dvādaśame varṣe punarbrāhmaṇatāṃ vrajet (39)|
Vai 323.005 iti niḥsaraṇaṃ dṛṣṭaṃ brāhmaṇaistu tapasvibhiḥ |
Vai 323.006 kumārgagāmibhirmūḍhairaniḥsaraṇadarśābhiḥ (40)|
Vai 323.007 taditdaṃ brāhmaṇa te bravīmi—saṃjñāmātrakamidaṃ lokasya yadidamucyate brāhmaṇa iti vā kṣatriya iti vā vaiśya iti vā śūdra iti vā |
Vai 323.008 sarvamidamekameveti vijñāya putrāya me śārdūlakarṇāya prakṛtiṃ māṇavikāmanuprayaccha bhāryārthāya |
Vai 323.009 yāvantaṃ kulaśulkaṃ manyase tāvantamanupradāsyāmi |
|
Vai 323.010 idaṃ ca khalu punarvacanaṃ śrutvā triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasya brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī abhiṣaktaḥ kupitaścaṇḍībhūto ’nāttamanāḥ kopaṃ ca dveṣaṃ ca tatpratyayaṃ janayitvā lalāṭe triśikhāṃ bhṛkuṭiṃ kṛtvā kaṇṭhaṃ dhamayitvā akṣiṇī parivartya nakulapiṅgalāṃ dṛṣṭimutpādya triśaṅkuṃ mātaṅgarājamidamavocat—Vai 323.013 asamīkṣyaitattvayā hi kṛtā saṃjñeyamīdṛśī |
Vai 323.014 ekaiva jātirloke ’smin sāmānyā na pṛthagvidhā (41)|
Vai 323.015 kathaṃ śvapākajātīyo brāhmaṇaṃ vedapāragam |
Vai 323.016 nihīnayonijo bhūtvā vimarditumihecchasi (42)|
Vai 323.017 rājānaḥ khalu vṛṣala prativibhāgajñā bhavanti |
tadyathā deśadharme vā nagaradharme vā grāmadharme vā nigamadharme vā śulkadharme vā āvāhadharme vā vivāhadharme vā pūrvakarmasu vā |
Vai 323.019 catvāra ime vṛṣala varṇāḥ |
yaduta brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdra iti |
teṣāṃ vivāhadharmeṣu catasro bhāryā brāhmaṇasya bhavanti |
Vai 323.020 tadyathā brāhmaṇī kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrī ceti |
tisraḥ kṣatriyasya bhāryā bhavanti |
Vai 323.021 kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrī ceti |
vaiśyasya dve bhārye bhavataḥ |
vaiśyā śūdrī ceti |
Vai 323.022 śūdrasya tvekā bhāryā bhavati śūdrī eva |
evaṃ brāhmaṇasya vṛṣala catvāraḥ putrā bhavanti |
Vai 323.023 tadyathā brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdraśceti |
kṣatriyasya trayaḥ putrāḥ, kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdra iti |
Vai 323.024 vaiśyasy dvau putrau, vaiśyaḥ śūdra iti |
śūdrasya tveka eva putro bhavati yaduta śūdra eva |
te brāhmaṇāḥ punarvṛṣala brāhmaṇaḥ putrāḥ |
Vai 323.025 aurasā mukhato jātāḥ |
urasto bāhutaḥ kṣatriyāḥ |
Vai 323.026 nābhito vaiśyāḥ |
padbhyāṃ śūdrāḥ |
brahmaṇāyaṃ khalu vṛṣala lokaḥ sarvabhūtāni nirmitāni |
Vai 323.027 tasya jyeṣṭhā vayaṃ putrāḥ kṣatriyāstadanantaram |
Vai 323.028 vaiśyāstṛtīyakā varṇāḥ śūdranāṃnā caturthakaḥ (43)|
iti |
|
Vai 323.029 sa tvaṃ vṛṣala caturthe ’pi varṇe na saṃdṛśase |
ahaṃ cāgre varṇe śreṣṭhe varṇe parame varṇe pravare varṇe |
Vai 323.030 paramārthaṃ ca samyogamākāṅkṣasi |
praṇaśya tvaṃ vṛṣala kṣipram |
mā cāsmākamavamaṃsthāḥ |
|
Vai 323.031 idaṃ punarvacanaṃ śrutvā brāhmaṇasya puṣkarasāriṇastriśaṅkurmātaṅgarāja idamavocat—idamatra brāhmaṇa śṛṇu yad bravīmi |
Vai 323.032 brahmaṇāyaṃ lokaḥ, sarvabhūtāni nirmitāni |
tasya jyeṣṭho vayaṃ putrāḥ kṣatriyāstadanantaram |
Vai 324.002 vaiśyāstṛtīyakā varṇāḥ śūdranāṃnā catruthakaḥ (44)|
iti |
|
Vai 324.003 sapādajaṅghāḥ sanakhāḥ samāṃsāḥ sapārśvapaṛṣṭhāśca narā bhavanti |
Vai 324.005 ekāṃśato nāsti yato viśeṣo varṇāśca catvāra ito na santi (45)|
Vai 324.007 atho viśeṣaḥ pravaro ’sti kaścittad brūhi yaccānumatam yathā te |
Vai 324.009 atho viśeṣaḥ pravaro hi nāsti varṇāśca catvāra ito na santi (46)|
Vai 324.011 yathā hi dārakā bālāḥ krīḍamānā mahāpathe |
Vai 324.012 pāṃśupuñjāni saṃpaṇḍya svayaṃ nāmāni kurvate (47)|
Vai 324.013 idaṃ kṣīramidaṃ dadhi idaṃ māṃsamidaṃ ghṛtam |
Vai 324.014 na ca bālasya vacanātpāṃśavo ’nnaṃ bhavanti hi (48)|
Vai 324.015 varṇāstathaiva catvāro yathā brāhmaṇa bhāṣase |
Vai 324.016 pāṃśupuñjābhidhānena yogo ’yaḥ kopyeṣa na vidyate (49)|
Vai 324.017 na keśena na karṇābhyāṃ na śīrṣeṇa na cakṣuṣā |
Vai 324.018 na mukhena na nāsayā na grīvayā na bāhunā (50)|
Vai 324.019 norasāpyatha pārśvābhyāṃ na pṛṣṭhenodareṇa ca |
Vai 324.020 norubhyāmatha jaṅghābhyāṃ pāṇipādanakhena ca (51)|
Vai 324.021 na svareṇa na varṇena na sarvāṃśair na maithunaiḥ |
Vai 324.022 nānāviśeṣaḥ sarveṣu manuṣyeṣu hi vidyate (52)|
Vai 324.023 yathā hi jātiṣvanyāsu liṅgam yoniḥ pṛthak pṛthak |
Vai 324.024 sāmānyaṃ kāraṇaṃ tatra kiṃ vā jātiṣu manyase (53)|
Vai 324.025 saśīrṣakāścātha narāsthiyuktāḥ sacarmakāḥ sendriyasodarāśca |
Vai 324.027 varṇā na yuktāścaturo ’bhidhātum (54)|
Vai 324.029 doṣo hyayaṃ cātra bhavedayukto yadyattvayā cābhihitaṃ nidāne |
Vai 324.031 śrutvā tu mattaḥ pratipadya saumya yaccātra manye śṛṇu codyamānam (55)|
yaccātra yuktaṃ viṣamaṃ samaṃ vā tatte pravakṣyāmi niyujyamānaḥ |
Vai 325.003 doṣo hi yaścāpi bhavedayukto vakṣyāmi te hyuttaratottaraṃ ca |
Vai 325.005 śrutvā tu mattaḥ pratipadya saumya karmādhipatyaprabhavā manuṣyāḥ (56)|
Vai 325.007 anumānamapi te brāhmaṇa yadi pramāṇam, tatra yad bravīṣi—brahmā eka iti tasmātprajā api ekajātyā eva |
Vai 325.008 vayamapyekajātyā bhavāmaḥ |
yacca bravīṣi—brahmaṇāyaṃ lokaḥ sarvabhūtāni ca nirmitānīti |
Vai 325.009 sacette brāhmaṇa idaṃ pramaṇam, tadidaṃ te brāhmaṇa ayuktam yad bravīṣi catvāro varṇāh—brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā śūdrāśceti |
Vai 325.010 api tu brāhmaṇa mithyā mama vaco bhavet, yadi brāhmaṇa saṃvādena manuṣyajāter nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.011 yaduta śīrṣato vā mukhato vā karṇato vā nāsikāto vā bhrūto vā rūpato vā saṃsthānato vā varṇato vā ākārato vā yonito vā āhārato vā saṃbhavato vā nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
|
Vai 325.014 tadyathāpi bhoḥ puṣkarasārin gavāśvagardabhoṣṭramṛgapakṣyajaiḍakānāmaṇḍajajarāyujasaṃsvedajaupapādukānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.015 yaduta pādato ’pi mukhato ’pi varṇato ’pi saṃsthānato ’pi āhārato ’pi yonisambhavato ’pi nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.016 na caivaṃ teṣāṃ caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.017 tattasmātsarvamidamekamiti |
|
Vai 325.018 api ca brāhmaṇa amīṣāṃ phalguvṛkṣāṇāmāmrātakajambukharjūrapanasadālāvanatindukamṛdvīkabījapūrakakapitthākṣoḍanārikelatiniśakarañjādīnāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.019 yaduta mūlataśca skandhataśca tvagbhāgataśca sārataśca patrataśca puṣpataśca phalataśca nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.020 na caivaṃ caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
|
Vai 325.022 tadyathā brāhmaṇa amīṣāṃ sthalajānāṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ sāratamālanaktamālakarṇikārasaptaparṇaśirīṣakovidārasyandanacandanaśiṃśapairaṇḍakhadirādīnāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.023 yaduta mūlataśca skandhataśca tvagbhāgataśca gulmataśca sārataśca patrataśca phalataśca viśeṣa upalabhyate |
Vai 325.024 na caivaṃ caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
|
Vai 325.026 tadyathā bhoḥ puṣkarasārin, amīṣāṃ kṣīravṛkṣāṇāmudumbaraplakṣāśvatthanayagrodhavalguketyevamādīnāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.027 yaduta mūlataśca skandhataśca tvagbhāgataśca sārataśca patrataśca puṣpataśca phalataśca nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.028 na tvena caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
|
Vai 325.029 tadyathā puṣkarasārin, amīṣāmapi phalabhaiṣajyavṛkṣāṇāmāmalakīharītakīvibhītakīpharasakādīnāmanyāsāmapi vividhānāmoṣadhīnāṃ grāmajānāṃ pārvatīyānāṃ tṛṇavanaspatīnāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 325.031 yaduta mūlataśca skandhataśca gulmataśca sārataśca patrataśca puṣpataśca phalataśca nānākaraṇaṃ prajāyate |
Vai 325.032 na tveva caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
|
tadyathā sthalajānāṃ puṣpavṛkṣāṇāmatimuktakacampakapāṭalānāṃ sumanāvārṣikādhanuṣkārikādīnāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 326.002 yaduta rūpato ’pi varṇato ’pi gandhato ’pi saṃsthānato ’pi nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 326.003 na tveva caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
|
Vai 326.004 tadyathā brāhmaṇa amīṣāmapi jalajānāṃ puṣpāṇāṃ padmotpalasaugandhakamṛdugandhikādīnāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
Vai 326.005 yaduta rūpataśca gandhataśca saṃsthānataśca varṇataśca nānākaraṇaṃ parjñāyate |
Vai 326.006 na tveva caturṇāṃ varṇānāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate |
tadyathā puṣkarasārinn amī brāhmaṇā iti kṣatriyā iti vaiśyā iti śūdrā iti |
Vai 326.007 tasmādekamevedaṃ sarvamiti |
|
Vai 326.008 apyanyatte pravakṣyāmi brāhmaṇaiḥ kalpitam yathā |
Vai 326.009 śiraḥ satāraṃ gaganamākāśamudaraṃ tathā (57)|
Vai 326.010 parvatāścāpyubhāvūrū pādau ca dharaṇītalam |
Vai 326.011 sūryācandramasau netre roma tṛṇavanaspatī (58)|
Vai 326.012 aśrūṇyavocadvarṣāsya nadyaḥ prasrāvameva ca |
Vai 326.013 sāgarāścāpyamedhyaṃ vai evaṃ braṃhā prajāpatiḥ (59)|
Vai 326.014 parīkṣasva tvaṃ brahmaṇaḥ svalakṣaṇam |
yasmād brahmaṇo brāhmaṇā utpannāḥ, tasmātkṣatriyā api vaiśyā api śūdrā apyutpannāḥ |
|
Vai 326.016 evaṃ prasūtiryadi tattvataḥ syāttato hi syādvarṇakṛto viśeṣaḥ |
Vai 326.018 yadi brāhmaṇā brahmalokaṃ vrajeyustrayaśca varṇā na vrajeyuḥ svargam |
Vai 326.020 evaṃ bhavedvarṇakṛto viśeṣo na cenna catvāro bhavanti varṇāḥ (60)|
Vai 326.022 yasmāddhi varṇaścaturtha evaṃ prayāti svargaṃ svakṛtena karmaṇā |
Vai 326.024 yatastapaścārṣamiha praśastaṃ tasmād dvijāter na viśeṣaṇaṃ syād (61)|
Vai 326.026 yadi brāhmaṇaḥ syādihaika eva dvijihvaścatuḥśravaṇastathaiva |
Vai 326.028 caturviṣāṇo bahupād dviśīrṣa evaṃ kṛte varṇakṛto viśeṣaḥ (62)|
rāgaiśca nāma paraghātanaṃ ca evamprakāraṃ ca viheṭhanaṃ ca |
Vai 327.003 sattvasya vai karmaṇo dhvaṃsanaṃ ca etānyakalyāṇakṛtāni vipraiḥ (63)|
Vai 327.005 yuddhaṃ vivādaṃ kalahānyabhīkṣṇaṃ goprokṣaṇaṃ cintitaṃ brāhmaṇairhi |
Vai 327.007 atharvaṇaṃ karmaṇā trāsanaṃ ca etāni mantrāṇi kṛtāni vipraiḥ (64)|
Vai 327.009 pāpecchatā bahujanavañcanaṃ ca śāṭhyaṃ ca dhauryaṃ ca tathaiva kalpam |
Vai 327.011 evaṃ pareṣāmahitaṃ vicintya kadā ca te svargamito vrajeyuḥ (65)|
Vai 327.013 ye brāhmaṇā ugratapā vinītā vratena śīlena sadā hyupetāḥ |
Vai 327.015 ahiṃsakā ye damasamyame ratāste brāhmaṇā brahmapuraṃ vrajanti (66)|
Vai 327.017 sahāsthimāṃsaḥ sanakhaḥ sacarmā duḥkhaṃ sukhaṃ mūtrapurīṣamekam |
Vai 327.019 pañcendriyair nāsti yato viśeṣastasmānna vai varṇacatuṣka eṣaḥ (67)|
Vai 327.021 tadyathā nāma brāhmaṇa kasyacitpuruṣasya catvāraḥ putrā bhaveyuḥ |
sa teṣāṃ nāmāni kuryāt—nandaka iti vā jīvaka iti vā aśoka iti vā śatāyuriti vā |
Vai 327.022 iṣṭāśca punarbho etasya puruṣasya putrā bhaveyuḥ |
Vai 327.023 tatra yo nandakaḥ sa nandet |
yo jīvakaḥ sa jīvet |
Vai 327.024 yo ’śokaḥ sa na śocet |
yaḥ śatāyuḥ sa varṣaśataṃ jīvet |
|
Vai 327.025 nāmataḥ punarbrāhmaṇa teṣāṃ nānākaraṇaṃ prajñāyate na jātitaḥ |
tatkasya hetoh? iha khalu punarbrahmaṇa pitṛtaḥ putro jāyate |
Vai 327.026 tasmācca tatredaṃ vyākaraṇaṃ bhavati—Vai 327.027 mātā bhastrā pituḥ putro yena jātaḥ sa eva saḥ |
Vai 327.028 yadyevaṃ bho vijānāsi na te (putrā) parabhūtāḥ kvacit (68)|
Vai 327.029 parīkṣasva brāhmaṇa samyageva—ko ’tra brāhmaṇaḥ kṣatriyo vaiśyaḥ śūdra iti |
Vai 327.030 sarve kāṇāśca kubjāśca sarve ’pasmāriṇo ’pi vā |
Vai 327.031 kilāsinaḥ kuṣṭhinaśca gaurāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ pṛthak pṛthak (69)|
pratiṣṭhitāḥ |
|
Vai 328.002 samamajjānakhatvacapārścodaravaktrāḥ prajā hi tāḥ svakarmaṇā |
Vai 328.003 evaṃ gate brāhmaṇa naiva bhavati viśeṣaḥ ko jātikṛto viśeṣaḥ |
Vai 328.004 yasmānna jāterviśeṣaṇo ’sti tasmānna vai varṇacatuṣka eva (69)|
(a)Vai 328.005 tasmātte brāhmaṇa bravīmi—saṃjñāmātramidaṃ lokasya yadidaṃ brāṃhaṇa iti vā kṣatriya iti vā vaiśya iti vā śūdra iti vā caṇḍāka iti vā |
Vai 328.006 ekamidaṃ sarvamidamekam |
putrāya me śārdūlakarṇāya prakṛtiṃ duhitaramutsṛja bhāryārthāya |
Vai 328.007 yāvantaṃ kulaśulkaṃ manyase tāvantamanupradāsyāmi |
|
Vai 328.008 idaṃ punarvacanaṃ śrutvā triśaṅkormātaṅgarājāsya brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī idamavocat—kiṃ punarbhavatā ṛgvedo ’dhītaḥ, yajurvedo ’dhītaḥ, sāmavedo ’dhītaḥ, arthavavedo ’dhītaḥ, āyurvedo ’dhītaḥ, kalpādhyāyo ’pi, adhyātmamapi, mṛgacakraṃ vā, nakṣatragaṇo vā, tithikramagaṇo vā tvayādhītah? karmacakraṃ vā tvayādhigatam? athavā aṅgavidyā vā vastravidyā vā śivāvidyā śakunividyā vā tvayādhītā? athavā rāhucaritaṃ vā śukracaritaṃ vā grahacaritaṃ tvayādhītam? athavā lokāyataṃ bhavatā bhāṣyapravacanaṃ vā pakṣādhyāyo vā nyāyo vā tvayādhītah?Vai 328.014 evamukte triśaṅkurmātaṅgarājaḥ puṣkarasāriṇaṃ brāhmaṇametadavocat—etacca mayā brāhmaṇā adhītaṃ bhūyaścottaram |
Vai 328.015 bhūyaścottaram |
yadapi te brāhmaṇa evaṃ syāt—ahamasmi mantreṣu pāraṃ prāpta iti, tatra te brāhmaṇa saha dharmeṇānumānaṃ pravakṣyāmi |
Vai 328.016 na khalvevaṃ brāhmaṇa prāthamakalpikānāṃ sattvānāmetadabhavat—yaduta brāhmaṇa iti vā kṣatriya iti vā vaiśya iti vā śūdra iti vā |
Vai 328.017 ekamidaṃ sarvamidamekam |
|
Vai 328.019 atha brāhmaṇa sattvānāmasadṛśānāṃ cobhayathā sadṛśānāṃ tato ’nye sattvāḥ śālikṣetrāṇi kelāyanti gopāyanti vāpayanti vā, te ’mī kṣatriyā iti saṃjñā udapādi |
Vai 328.020 athātra brāhmaṇa tadanyatamānāṃ sattvānāmetadabhavat—parigraho rogaḥ parigraho gaṇḍaḥ parigrahaḥ śalyaḥ |
Vai 328.021 yannu vayaṃ svaparigrahamapahāya araṇyāyatanaṃ gatvā tṛṇakāṣṭhaśākhāparṇapalāśakānupasaṃhṛtya tṛṇakuṭikāṃ vā parṇakuṭikāṃ vā kṛtvā praviśya dhyāyema iti |
Vai 328.023 atha te sattvāstaṃ parigrahamapahāyā araṇyāyatanaṃ gatvā tṛṇakāṣṭhaśākhāpatraparṇapālāśakaistṛṇakuṭiṃ vā parṇakuṭikāṃ vā kṛtvā tatraiva praviśya dhyāyanti sma |
Vai 328.025 te tatra sāyamāsanahetoḥ prāntavāṭikāṃ prātaraśanahetośca grāmaṃ piṇḍāya praviśanti sma |
|
Vai 328.027 atha teṣāṃ grāmavāsināṃ satvānāmetadabhavat—duṣkarakārakā bata bhoḥ sattvā ye svakaṃ parigrahamutsṛjya grāmanigamajanapadebhyo bahir nirgatāḥ |
Vai 328.028 teṣāṃ bahirmanaskā brāhmaṇā iti saṃjñā udapādi |
Vai 328.029 te ca punargrāmavāsinaḥ sattvāstānatīva satkurvanti sma |
teṣāṃ ca dātavyaṃ manyante sma |
|
atha etṣāmeva sattvānāmanyatame sattvāstāni dhyānānyasambhāvayanto grāmeṣvavatīrya mantrapadān svādhyāyanti sma |
Vai 329.002 tāṃste grāmanivāsina āhuh—na kevalamime sattvāḥ, ime ’dhyāpakāḥ, teṣāmadhyāpakā iti loke saṃjñā udapādi |
Vai 329.003 ayaṃ heturayaṃ pratyayo brāhmaṇānāṃ loke prādurbhāvāya |
|
Vai 329.005 athānyatame sattvā vivekakālapratisamyuktān kārmāntān vividhānarthapratisamyuktān kurvanti sma |
Vai 329.006 teṣāṃ vaiśyā iti saṃjñā udapādi |
|
Vai 329.007 athānyatame sattvāḥ kṣudreṇa karmaṇā jīvikāṃ kalpayanti sma |
teṣāṃ śūdrā iti saṃjñā udapādi |
|
Vai 329.009 bhūtapūrvaṃ brāhmaṇa anyatamaḥ sattvo vadhūmādāya rathamāruhya anyatamasminnaraṇyapradeśe gataḥ |
Vai 329.010 tatra ca ratho bhagnaḥ |
tasmānmātaṅgam mā tvaṃ gāmah iti saṃjñā udapādi |
|
Vai 329.011 kṣetraṃ karṣanti ye teṣāṃ karṣakā iti saṃjñā pravṛttā |
|
Vai 329.012 bhāṣyeṇa ca parṣadaṃ rañjayati dharmeṇa śīlavratasamācāreṇa samyak, tasya rājā iti saṃjñābhūt |
|
Vai 329.014 tato ’nye sattvā vāṇijyayā jīvikāṃ kalpayanti, teṣāṃ vaṇija iti saṃjñā udapādi |
|
Vai 329.015 tataścānye sattvāḥ pravrajanti sma |
pravrajitvā parāñ jayanti kleśāñ jayantīti teṣāṃ pravrajitā iti loke saṃjñā udapādi |
|
Vai 329.017 api tu brāhmaṇa ekaiva saṃjñā loka udapādi |
tāṃ te pravakṣyāmi—Vai 329.018 brahmā loke ’sminn imān vedān vācayati |
brahmā devānāṃ paramatāpasaḥ |
indrasya kauśikasya vedān vācayati sma |
Vai 329.019 indraḥ kauśiko ’raṇemi—gautamaṃ vedān vācayati |
araṇemi—gautamaḥ śvetaketuṃ vedān vācayati |
Vai 329.020 śvetaketuḥ śukaṃ paṇḍitaṃ vācayati |
śukaḥ paṇḍitaśca vedān vibhajati sma |
Vai 329.021 tadyathā puṣyo bahvṛcānāṃ paṅktiśchandogānāmekaviṃśatiradhvaryavaḥ |
Vai 329.022 kraturatharvāṇikānām |
ba ṛ??? cānāmete brāhmaṇa |
sarve te vyākhyāyante |
puṣya eko bhūtvā pañcaviṃśatidhā bhinnaḥ |
Vai 329.023 tadyathā śuklā valkalā māṇḍavyā iti |
tatra daśa śuklāḥ |
aṣṭau valkalāḥ |
Vai 329.024 sapta māṇḍavyāḥ |
itīyaṃ brāhmaṇa bahvṛcānāṃ śākhā |
puṣya eko bhūtvā pañcaviṃśatidhā bhinnaḥ |
|
Vai 329.026 anumānamapi brāhmaṇa pramāṇaṃ chandogānām |
brāhmaṇāḥ sarva ete chandogāḥ |
paṅktirityekā bhūtvā sāśītisahasradhā bhinnā |
Vai 329.027 tadyathā śīlavalkā araṇemikā laukākṣāḥ kauthumā brahmasamā mahāsamā mahāyāgikāḥ sātyamugrāḥ samantavedāḥ |
|
Vai 329.029 tatra śīlavalkā viṃśatiḥ |
araṇemikā viṃśatiḥ |
laukākṣāścatvāriṃśat |
kauthumānāṃ śatam |
Vai 329.030 brahmasamānāṃ śatam |
sātyamugrāṇāṃ śatam |
Vai 329.031 samantavedānāṃ śatam |
itīyaṃ brāhmaṇa cchandoganāṃ śākhā |
paṅktirityekā bhūtvā sāśītisahasradhā bhinnā |
|
anumānamapi pramāṇamadhvaryūṇām |
Vai 330.001 ete brāhmaṇā ekaviṃśatyadhvaryavo bhūtvā ekottaraśatadhā bhinnāḥ |
Vai 330.002 tadyathā kaṭhāḥ kaṇimā vājasaneyino jātukarṇāḥ praṣṭhapadā ṛṣayaḥ |
tatra daśa kaṭhāḥ |
Vai 330.003 daśa kaṇimāḥ |
ekādaśa vājasaneyinaḥ |
trayodaśa jātukarṇāḥ |
ṣoḍaśa ṣoṣṭhapadāḥ |
Vai 330.004 ekacatvāriṃśadṛṣayaḥ |
itīyaṃ brāhmaṇa adhvaryūṇāṃ śākhā |
ekaviṃśatyadhvaryavo bhūtvā ekottaraśatadhā bhinnāḥ |
|
Vai 330.006 anumānamapi brāhmaṇa pramāṇamatharvaṇikānām |
ete mantrāḥ sarve te ’tharvaṇikāḥ |
Vai 330.007 kratureko bhūtvā dvidhā bhinnaḥ |
caturdhā bhūtvā aṣṭadhā bhinnaḥ |
Vai 330.008 aṣṭadhā bhūtvā navadaśadhā bhinnaḥ |
itīyaṃ brahmaṇa arharvaṇikānāṃ śākhā |
kraturekaḥ ṣoḍaśottaradvādaśaśatadhā bhinnaḥ |
|
Vai 330.010 anumānamapi brāhmaṇa pramāṇaṃ pratītya etāni dvādaśabhedaśatāni ṣoḍaśabhedāśca ye brāhmaṇaiḥ pauraṇaiḥ samyag dṛṣṭāḥ |
Vai 330.011 chandasi vā vyākaraṇe vā lokayate vā padamīmāṃsāyāṃ vā |
Vai 330.012 na caiṣāmūhāpohaḥ prajñāyate |
yaduta ekajātyo nāmeti viditvā bandhurbhavitumarhati |
tatte brāhmaṇa bravīmi—saṃjñāmātrakametallokasya yaduta brāhmaṇa iti vā kṣatriya iti vā vaśya iti vā śūdra iti vā |
Vai 330.014 ekamidaṃ sarvamidamekam |
putrāya me śārdūlakarṇāya prakṛtiṃ duhitamutsṛja bhāryārthāya |
Vai 330.015 yāvantaṃ kulaśulkaṃ manyase tāvantamanupradāsyāmi |
|
Vai 330.016 idaṃ punarvacanaṃ śrutvā triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasya brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī tūṣṇīmbhūto madgubhūtaḥ srastaskandho ’dhomukho niṣpratibhaḥ pradhyānaparo ’sthāt |
|
Vai 330.018 dadarśa triśaṅkurmātaṅgarājo brāhmaṇaṃ puṣkarasāriṇaṃ tūṣṇīmbhūtaṃ madgubhūtaṃ srastaskandhamadhomukhaṃ niṣpratibhaṃ pradhyānaparaṃ sthitam |
Vai 330.019 dṛṣṭvā ca punaridamabravīt—yadapi te brāhmaṇa evaṃ syādasadṛśena saha saṃbandho bhaviṣyatīti |
Vai 330.020 na punastvayā brāhmaṇa evaṃ draṣṭavyam |
tatkasya hetoh? ye pramāṇaśrutiśīlaprajñādayo guṇā agryā lokasya te mama putrasya śārdūlakarṇasya saṃvidyante |
Vai 330.022 yadapi te brāhmaṇa evaṃ syāt—ye vājapeyam yajñam yajanti, aśvamedhaṃ puruṣamedhaṃ śāmyaprāśaṃ nirargaḍam yajñam yajanti, sarve te kāyasya bhedātsugatau svargaloke deveṣūpapadyanta iti |
Vai 330.024 na punarbrāhmaṇa tvayaivaṃ draṣṭavyam |
tatkasya hetoh? vājapeyaṃ brāhmaṇa yajñam yajamānā aśvamedhaṃ puruṣamedhaṃ śāmyaprāśaṃ nirargaḍam yajña ca yajamānā bahudhā mantrān pravartayantaḥ prāṇihiṃsāṃ ca pravartayanti |
Vai 330.026 tasmātte brāhmaṇa bravīmi—na hyeṣa mārgaḥ svargāya |
ahaṃ te brāhmaṇa mārgaṃ svargāya vyākhyāmi |
Vai 330.027 tacchṛṇu—Vai 330.028 śīlaṃ rakṣeta medhāvī prārthayānaḥ sukhatrayam |
Vai 330.029 praśaṃsāṃ vittalābhaṃ ca pratya svarge ca modanam (70)|
Vai 330.030 yairbrāhmaṇa itaḥ pūrvaṃ vājapeyo yajña iṣṭaḥ, yairaśvamedho yaiḥ puruṣamedho yaiḥ śāmyaprāśo yair nirargaḍo yajña iṣṭaḥ, parigṛhītastair nirargalaṃ ca kāmaiḥ kāmaḥ |
Vai 330.031 ito nākaḥ paryeṣyate |
ye Vai 331.000brāhmaṇa itaḥ paścādvājapeyam yajñam yakṣyanti, ye ’śvamedham ye śāmyaprāśaṃ nirargaḍam yajñam yakṣyanti, te nirarthakaṃ mahāvighātaṃ samyokṣyanti |
Vai 331.002 tasmātte brāhmaṇa bravīmi—ehi tvaṃ mayā sārdhaṃ saṃbandham yojanayasva |
Vai 331.003 tatkasya hetoh? dharmeṇa hi caṇḍālā ajugupsanīyā bhavanti |
Vai 331.004 api ca |
Vai 331.005 śraddhā śīlaṃ tapastyāgaḥ śrutirjñānaṃ dayaiva ca |
|
Vai 331.006 darśanaṃ sarvavedānāṃ svargavratapadāni vai (71)|
Vai 331.007 pramāṇamaṣṭaprakāraṃ svargāya |
Vai 331.008 tadebhiraṣṭābhiḥ prakārair dvargagamanamiṣyate |
ye prāyeṇa jānanti viśeṣeṇa khalvapyanekairvividhairyajñaiḥ |
aṣṭau cemā brāhmaṇa nirdiṣṭā mātṛtulyā bhaginyo loke pravartante |

duturdānavānām |
manurmānavānām |

mahākāśyapaṃ manasā vidanti ṛṣayaḥ |
|
Vai 331.012 atha khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin brāhmaṇānāṃ sapta gautrāṇi svākhyāsyāmi, tāni śrūyantām—tadyathā gautamā vātsyāḥ kautsāḥ kāśyapā vāsiṣṭhā māṇḍavyā ityetāni brāhmaṇa sapta gotrāṇi |
Vai 331.014 eṣāmekaikaṃ gotraṃ saptadhā bhinnam |
atra ye gautamāste kauthumāste gagarste bhāradvājāsta ārṣṭiṣeṇāste vaikhānasāste vajrapādāḥ |
Vai 331.015 tatra ye vātsyāsta ātreyāste maitreyāste bhārgavāste sāvarṇyāste bahujātāḥ |
Vai 331.016 tatra ye vātsyāsta ātreyāsta maitreyāste bhārgavāste sāvarṇyāste salīlāste bahujātāḥ |

) |
Vai 331.018 tatra ye kāśyapāste maṇḍanāsta iṣṭāste śauṇḍāyanāste rocaneyāste ’napekṣāste ’gniveśyāḥ |
Vai 331.019 tatra ye kāśyapāste jātukarṇyāste dhānyāyanāste pārāśarāste vyāghranakhāste āṇḍāyanāsta aupamanyavāḥ |
Vai 331.021 tatra ye māṇḍavyāste bhāṇḍāyanāste dhomrāyaṇāste kātyāyanāste khalvavāahanāste sugandhārāyaṇāste kāpiṣṭhalāyanāḥ |
Vai 331.022 ityetāni brāhmaṇa evamekonapañcāśadgotrāṇi brāhmaṇaiḥ paurāṇaiḥ samyag dṛṣṭāni cchandasi vyākaraṇe padamīmāṃsāyām |
Vai 331.023 anyāni ca gotrāṇi vistarato mayā vācitāni |
Vai 331.024 tāni anyair na jñāyante |
|
Vai 331.025 yadutaikatvamiti viditvā bhavān bandhurbhavitumarhati |
tasmātte brāhmaṇa bravīmi sāmānyaṃ saṃjñāmātrakamidaṃ lokasya yaduta brāhmaṇa iti vā kṣatriya iti vā vaiśya iti vā śūdra iti vā |
Vai 331.027 ekamidaṃ sarvamidamekam |
putrāya me śārdūlakarṇāya prakṛtiṃ duhitaramutsṛja bhāryārthāya |
Vai 331.028 yāvantaṃ kulaśulkaṃ manyase tāvantamanupradāsyāmi |
|
Vai 331.029 idaṃ punarvacanaṃ śrutvā triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasya brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī tūṣṇīmbhūto madgubhūtaḥ srastaskandho ’dhomukho niṣpratibhaḥ pradhyānaparaḥ sthito ’bhūt |
Vai 331.030 adrākṣīt triśaṅkurmātaṅgarājah Vai 332.000puskarasāriṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ tūṣṇīmbhūtaṃ madgubhūtaṃ srastaskandhamadhomukhaṃ niṣpratibhaṃ pradhyānaparaṃ sthitam |
dṛṣṭvā ca punaridamavocat—Vai 332.003 yādṛśaṃ vāpyate bījaṃ tādṛśaṃ labhyate phalam |
Vai 332.004 prajāpaterhi caikatve nirviśeṣo bhavatyataḥ (72)|
Vai 332.005 na cendriyāṇāṃ nānātvaṃ kriyābhedaśca dṛśyate |
Vai 332.006 brāhmaṇe vānyajātau vā naiṣāṃ kiṃcidviśiṣyate (73)|
Vai 332.007 na hyātmanaḥ samutlarṣaḥ śreṣṭhatvamiha yujyate |
Vai 332.008 śukraśoṇitasambhūtam yonito hyubhayaṃ samam (74)|
Vai 332.009 cāturvarṇyaṃ pravakṣyāmi paśudharmakathāṃ tava |
Vai 332.010 bhavette bhavinī bhāryā naitad brāhmaṇa yujyate (75)|
Vai 332.011 yadi tāvadayaṃ loko brahmaṇā janitaḥ svayam |
Vai 332.012 brāhmaṇī brāhmaṇasvasā kṣatriyā kṣatriyasvasāa (76)|
Vai 332.013 atha vaiśyasya vaiśyā vai śūdrā vā punaḥ |
Vai 332.014 na bhāryā bhaginī yuktā brahmaṇā janitā yadi (77)|
Vai 332.015 na sattvā brahmaṇo jātāḥ kleśajāḥ karmajāstvamī |
Vai 332.016 nīcaiścoccaiśca dṛśyante sattvā nānāśrayāḥ pṛthak (78)|
Vai 332.017 teṣāṃ ca jātisāmānyād brāhmaṇe kṣatriye tathā |
Vai 332.018 atha vaiśye ca śūdre ca samaṃ jñānaṃ pravartate (79)|
Vai 332.019 ṛgvedo ’tha yajurvedaḥ sāmavedo ’pyatharvaṇam |
Vai 332.020 itihāso nighaṇṭaśca kutaśchando nirarthakam (80)|
Vai 332.021 asmākamapyadhyayane maitrī vidyā tathā śikhī |

Vai 332.023 manojavā ca gāndhārī ghorī vidyā vaśaṃkarī |
Vai 332.024 kākavāṇī ca mantraṃ ca indrajālaṃ ca bhañjanī (82)|
Vai 332.025 asmākamāsītpuruṣā vidyāsvākhyātapaṇḍitāḥ |
Vai 332.026 maṇipuṣpāśca ṛṣayo bhāsvarāśca maharṣayaḥ (83)|
Vai 332.027 saṃlprāptā devatāṛddhiṃ kiṃ cikitsasi vidyayā |
Vai 332.028 aśikṣitāśca caṇḍālā brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ (84)|
Vai 332.029 kipiṃjalādyo janito mantrāṇāṃ pāramiṃ gataḥ |
Vai 332.030 na hyasau brāhmaṇīputraḥ kiṃ vā brāhmaṇa manyase (85)|
niṣadyajanayatkālī putraṃ dvaipāyanaṃ munim |
Vai 333.002 ugraṃ tejasvinaṃ bhīṣmaṃ pañcābhijñaṃ mahātapam |
Vai 333.003 na hyasau brāhmaṇīputraḥ kiṃ vā brāhmaṇa vakṣyasi (86)|
Vai 333.004 kṣatriyā reṇukā nāma jajñe rāmaṃ mahāmunim |
Vai 333.005 paṇḍitaṃ ca vinītaṃ ca sarvaśāstraviśāradam |
Vai 333.006 na hyasau brāhmaṇīputraḥ kiṃ vā brāhmaṇa vakṣyasi (87)|

Vai 333.008 paṇḍitāśca vinītāśca loke ca ṛṣisaṃmatāḥ |
Vai 333.009 na hi te brāhmaṇīputrāḥ kiṃ vā brāhmaṇa vakṣyasi (88)|
Vai 333.010 saṃjñā kṛteyaṃ lokasya brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāstathā |

Vai 333.012 tasmātte brāhmaṇa bravīmi saṃjñāmātrakamidaṃ lokasya yaduta brāhmaṇa iti vā kṣatriya iti vā vaiśya iti vā śūdra iti vā |

putrāya me śārdūlakarṇāya prakṛtiṃ duhitaramanuprayaccha bhāryārthāya |
Vai 333.014 yāvantaṃ kulaśulkaṃ manyase tāvantamanupradāsyāmi |
|
Vai 333.015 idaṃ ca punarvacanaṃ śrutvā triśaṅkormātaṅgarājasya brāhmaṇaḥ puṣkarasārī triśaṅkuṃ mātaṅgarājamidamavocat—kiṃgotro bhavān? āha—ātreyagotro ’smi |

Vai 335.009 anurādhānakṣatraṃ catustāraṃ ratnāvalīsaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ surāmāṃsāhāraṃ mitradaivatamālambāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |

Vai 335.011 mūlanakṣatraṃ saptatāraṃ vṛścikasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ mūlaphalāhāraṃ nairṛtidaivataṃ kātyāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.012 pūrvāṣāḍhānakṣatraṃ catustāraṃ govikramasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ nyagrodhakaṣāyāhāraṃ toyadaivataṃ darbhakātyāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.013 uttarāṣāḍhānakṣatraṃ catustāraṃ gajavikramasaṃsthānaṃ pañcacatvāriṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ madhulājāhāraṃ viśvadaivataṃ maudgalāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.015 abhijinnakṣatraṃ tritāraṃ gośīrṣasaṃsthānaṃ ṣaṇmuhūrtayogaṃ vāyvāhāraṃ brahmadaivataṃ brahmāvatīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.016 śravaṇānakṣatraṃ tritāram yavamadhyasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ pakṣimāṃsāhāraṃ viṣṇudaivataṃ kātyāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.017 ityetāni bhoḥ puṣkarasārin sapta nakṣatrāṇi paścimadvārakāṇi |
|
Vai 335.019 dhaniṣṭhānakṣatraṃ catustāraṃ śakunasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ kulatthapūpāhāraṃ vasudaivataṃ kauṇḍinyāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.020 śatabhiṣānakṣatramekatāraṃ tilakasaṃsthānaṃ pañcadaśamuhūrtayogam yavāgubhojanaṃ varuṇadaivataṃ tāṇḍyāyanīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.021 pūrvabhādrapadānakṣatraṃ dvitāraṃ padakasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ māṃsarudhirāhāramahirbudhnyadaivataṃ jātūkarṇyaṃ gotreṇa |

Vai 335.024 revatīnakṣatramekatāraṃ tilakasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ madhupāyasabhojanaṃ gandharvadaivataṃ maitrāyaṇīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.026 bharaṇīnakṣatraṃ tritāraṃ bhagasaṃsthānaṃ triṃśanmuhūrtayogaṃ tilataṇḍulāhāram yamadaivataṃ bhārgavīyaṃ gotreṇa |
Vai 335.027 ityetāni bhoḥ puṣkarasārin sapta nakṣatrāṇi uttaradvārakāṇi |
|
Vai 335.028 amīṣāṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aṣṭaviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ ṣaṇnakṣatrāṇi pañcacatvāriṃśanmuhūrtayogāni |
Vai 335.029 tadyathā—rohiṇī punarvasu uttaraphalgunī viśākhā uttarāṣāḍhā uttarabhādrapadā ceti |
Vai 335.030 pañcanakṣatrāṇi pañcadaśamuhūrtayogāni |
tadyathā—ārdrā āśleṣā svātī jyeṣṭhā śatabhiṣā ceti |
Vai 335.031 eko ’bhijit ṣaṇmuhūrtayogam |
avaśiṣṭāni triṃśanmuhūrtayogāni |
|

Vai 336.002 amīṣāṃ saptānāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ dakṣiṇadvārīkāṇāṃ maghā prathamā nāma, viśākhā paścimāa nāma |
Vai 336.003 amīṣāṃ paścimadvārikāṇāṃ saptānāṃ nakṣatrāṇāmanurādhā prathamā nāma, śravaṇā paścimā nāma |
Vai 336.004 amīṣāṃ saptānāṃ nakṣatrāṇāmuttaradvārikāṇāṃ dhaniṣṭhā prathamā nāma, bharaṇī paścimā nāma |

Vai 336.006 amīṣāṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aṣṭāviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ sapta balāni |

Vai 336.007 triṇi dāruṇāni |
ārdrā āśleṣā bharaṇī ceti |
Vai 336.008 catvāri saṃmānanīyāni |

pañca mṛdukāni |
Vai 336.009 śravaṇā dhaniṣṭhā śatabhiṣā jyeṣṭhā mūlā iti |
pañca dhāraṇīyāni |

Vai 336.010 catvāri kṣiprakaraṇīyāni |

|
Vai 336.011 amīṣāṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aṣṭhāviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ trayo yogā bhavanti—ṛṣabhānusārī yogaḥ |
Vai 336.012 vatsānusārī yogaḥ |
yuganaddho yogaḥ |
tatra nakṣatram yadi purastādgacchati candraśca pṛṣṭhataḥ, ayamucyate ṛṣabhānusārī yoga iti |
Vai 336.013 yaduta candraḥ purastād gacchati nakṣatraṃ ca pṛṣṭhataḥ, tadā bhavati vatsānusārī yogaḥ |
Vai 336.014 yadi punaścandro nakṣatraṃ cobhau samau yugapad gacchataḥ, tadāyamucyate yoga iti |
|
Vai 336.016 atha khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin grahān pravakṣyāmi |
tacchrūyatām |
tadyathā śukro bṛhaspatiḥ śanaiścaro budho ’ṅgārakaḥ sūryastārādhipatiśceti |
|
Vai 336.018 evaṃ viparivartamāne loke nakṣatreṣu pravibhakteṣu kathaṃ rātridivasānāṃ hrāso vṛddhiśca bhavati? taducyate |
Vai 336.019 hemantānāṃ dvitīye māsi rohiṇyāmaṣṭabhyāṃ dvādaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |
Vai 336.020 aṣṭādaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ |
grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse rohiṇyāmaṣṭabhyāmaṣṭādaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |
Vai 336.021 dvādaśamuhūrto rātriḥ |
varṣāṇāṃ paścime māse rohiṇyāmaṣṭabhyāṃ caturdaśamuhūrto divase bhavati |

|

Vai 336.025 kiṃ bhostriśaṅko kṣaṇasya parimāṇam? kiṃ lavāsya? kiṃ muhūrtasya? tadyathā bhoḥ puṣkarasārin striyā nātidīrghahrasvaḥ kartinyāḥ sūtrodyāmaḥ |

etena kramasambandhena triṃśanmuhūrtamekaṃ rātridivasamanumīyate |
Vai 336.028 teṣāṃ muhūrtānāmimāni nāmāni bhavanti—Vai 336.029 āditya udayati ṣaṇṇavatipauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ caturojā nāma muhūrto bhavati |

Vai 336.030 dvādaśapauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ samṛddho nāma muhūrto bhavati |
Vai 336.031 ṣaṭpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ śarapathe nāma muhūrto bhavati |
pañcapauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāmatisamṛddhoVai 337.000 nāma muhūrto bhavati |
Vai 337.001 catuḥpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāmudgato nāma muhūrto bhavati |
Vai 337.002 tripauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ sumukho nāma muhūrto bhavati |
sthite madhyāhne vajrako nāma muhūrto bhavati |
Vai 337.003 parivṛto madhyāhne tripuruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ rohito nāma muhūrto bhavati |
catuḥpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ balo muhūrtaḥ |
Vai 337.004 pañcapauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ vijayo nāma muhūrtaḥ |
ṣaṭpauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ sarvaraso nāma muhūrtaḥ |
Vai 337.005 dvādaśapauruṣāyāṃ chāyāyāṃ vasur nāma muhūrtaḥ |

|

Vai 337.015 tatkṣaṇaḥ kṣaṇo lavo muhūrtaḥ |
tatra triṃśatitamo bhāgo muhūrtasya lavaḥ |
ṣaṣṭitamo bhāgo lavasya kṣaṇaḥ |
Vai 337.016 viṃśatyuttarabhāgaśataṃ kṣaṇasya tatkṣaṇaḥ |
tadyathā striyā nātidīrghahrasvaḥ kartinyāḥ sūtrodyāmaḥ |
Vai 337.017 evaṃ dīrghastatkṣaṇaḥ |

ṣaṣṭiḥ kṣaṇā eko lavaḥ |
Vai 337.018 triṃśallavā eko muhūrtaḥ |
etena kramayogena triṃśanmuhūrtamekamahorātram |

dvādaśa māsāḥ saṃvatsaraḥ |
caturojāḥ śvetaḥ samṛddhaḥ śarapatho ’tisamṛddha udgataḥ sumukho vajrako rohito balo vijayaḥ sarvaraso vasuḥ sundaraḥ parabhayaḥ |
Vai 337.020 raudrastārāvacaraḥ samyamaḥ sāmpraiyako ’nanto gardabho rākṣaso ’vayavo brahmā ditirarko vidhamano āgneya ātapāgnirabhijit |
Vai 337.022 itīmāni muhūrtānāṃ nāmāni |
|
Vai 337.023 kālotpattimapi te brāhmaṇa vakṣyāmi, śṛṇu—Vai 337.024 kālasya kiṃ pramāṇamiti taducyate |

aṣṭau lavā ekā kāṣṭhā |
Vai 337.025 ṣoḍaśa kāṣṭhā ekā kalā |
kalānāṃ triṃśadekā nāḍikā |
tatra dve nāḍike eko muhūrtaḥ |
|
Vai 337.026 nāḍikāyāḥ punaḥ kiṃ pramāṇam? taducyate—Vai 337.027 droṇaṃ salilasyaikam |

nālikāchidrasya kiṃ pramāṇam? suvarṇamātram |

vṛttaparimaṇḍalā samantāccaturasrā āyatā |

Vai 338.003 etena punarakṣinimeṣeṇa ṣoḍaśakoṭyo ’ṣṭapañcāśañca śatasahasrāṇi aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi sa evaṃ māpitaḥ |

Vai 338.005 śṛṇu brāhmaṇa trośayojanānāmutpattim |
Vai 338.006 vātāyanarajāṃsi sapta, śaśakrajaḥ |

sapta yūkā ekā likṣā |
Vai 338.008 sapta likṣā eko yavaḥ |

dve vitastī eko hastaḥ |

dhanuḥsahasramekaḥ krośaḥ |

tatkathayatu bhavān—Vai 338.013 dvādaśa yavā māṣakaḥ |

Vai 338.018 evaṃ māpitaṃ brāhmaṇa palasya parimāṇamiti |

Vai 338.027 paṭha bhostriśaṅko nakṣatravyākaraṇaṃ nāmādhyāyam |

Vai 338.030 mṛgaśirasi jāto yuddhārthī bhavati |

āśleṣāyām Vai 339.000jātaḥ kāmuko bhavati |
Vai 339.001 maghāyāṃ jāto matimān bhavati, mahātmā ca |

Vai 339.004 svātyāṃ jāto gaṇako bhavati, gaṇakamahāmātro vā |

Vai 339.005 anurādhāyāṃ jāto vāṇijako bhavati sārthikaḥ |

Vai 339.006 mūle jātaḥ putravān bhavati, yaśasvī ca |
pūrvāṣāḍhāyāṃ jāto yogācāro bhavati |
Vai 339.007 uttarāṣāḍhāyāṃ jāto bhakteśvaraḥ kulīnaśca bhavati |

Vai 339.008 śravaṇe jāto rājapūrjito bhavati |

Vai 339.012 paṭha bhostriśaṅko nakṣatranirdeśaṃ nāmādhyāyam |

Vai 339.013 tacchrūyatām |
kathayatu bhavān—Vai 339.014 kṛttikāsu niviṣṭaṃ vai nagaraṃ jvalati śriyā |
Vai 339.015 prabhūtaratnojjvalaṃ caivaṃ tannagaraṃ vinirdiśet (92)|
Vai 339.016 rohiṇyāṃ tu niviṣṭaṃ vai nagaraṃ tad vinirdiśet |
Vai 339.017 dhārmiko ’tra jano bhūyātprabhūtadhanasaṃcayaḥ |
Vai 339.018 vidyāprakṛtisampannaḥ svadārābhirato ’pi ca (93)|
Vai 339.019 mṛgaśīrṣe niviṣṭaṃ tu strībhirgobhirdhanaistathā |
Vai 339.020 mālyabhogaiśca saṃkīrṇamadbhutaiśca puraskṛtam (94)|
Vai 339.021 ārdrāyāṃ matsyamāṃsāni bhakṣyabhojyadhanāni ca |
Vai 339.022 bhavanti krūrapuruṣā mūrkhaprakṛtayaḥ pure (95)|
Vai 339.023 punarvasau niviṣḍe tu nagaraṃ dīpyate śriyā |
Vai 339.024 prabhūtadhanadhānyaṃ ca bhūtvā cāpi viniśyati (96)|
Vai 339.025 śrīmatpuṣye niviṣṭe tu prajā duṣṭā prasīdati |
Vai 339.026 yuktāḥ śriyā ca dharmiṣḍhāstathaiva cirajīvinaḥ (97)|
Vai 339.027 tejasvinaśca dīrghāyurdhanadhānyarasānvitāḥ |
Vai 339.028 vanaspatistathā kṣipraṃ puṣyettatra punaḥ punaḥ (98)|
Vai 339.029 āśleṣāyāṃ niviṣṭe tu durbhagāḥ kalahapriyāḥ |
Vai 339.030 duḥśīlā duḥkhabhājaśca nivasanti narādhamāḥ (99)|
Vai 339.031 maghāyāṃ ca niviṣṭe tu vidyāvanto mahādhanāḥ |
Vai 339.032 svadārābhiratā martyā jāyante suparākramāḥ (100)|
phālgunyāṃ tu striyo mālyaṃ bhojanācchādanaṃ śubham |
Vai 340.002 gandhopetāni dhānyāni niviṣṭe nagare bhavet (101)|
Vai 340.003 uttarāyāṃ tu phalgunyāṃ dhānyāni ca dhanāni ca |
Vai 340.004 mūrkhā janā strībhir niviṣṭe nagare bhavet (102)|
Vai 340.005 haste ca viniviṣṭe tu vidyāvanto mahādhanāḥ |
Vai 340.006 parasparaṃ ca rucitaṃ śayanaṃ nagare bhavet (103)|
Vai 340.007 citrāyāṃ ca niviṣṭe tu strījitāḥ sarvamānavāḥ |
Vai 340.008 śrīmatkāntaṃ ca nagaraṃ jvalantaṃ tadvinirdiśet (104)|
Vai 340.009 svātyāṃ pure niviṣṭe tu prabhūtadhanasaṃcayāḥ |
Vai 340.010 lubdhāḥ krūrāśca mūrkhāśca prabhūtā nagare bhavet (105)|
Vai 340.011 viśākhāyāṃ niviṣṭaṃ tu nagaraṃ jvalati śriyā |
Vai 340.012 yāyajūkajanākīrṇaṃ śastrāntaṃ ca vinirdiśet (106)|
Vai 340.013 anurādhāniviṣṭe tu dharmaśīlā jitendriyāḥ |
Vai 340.014 svadāraniratāḥ puṇyā japahomaparāyaṇāḥ (107)|
Vai 340.015 jyeṣṭhāyāṃ saṃniviṣṭaṃ tu bahuratnadhanānvitaiḥ |
Vai 340.016 sattvairvedavidaiḥ pūrṇaṃ śaśvatsamabhivardhate (108)|
Vai 340.017 mūlena saṃniviṣṭaṃ tu puraṃ dhānyadhanānvitam |
Vai 340.018 duḥśīlajanasaṃkīrṇaṃ pāṃsunā ca vinaśyati (109)|
Vai 340.019 pūrvāṣāḍhāniviṣṭaṃ tu puraṃ syāddhanadhānyabhāk |
Vai 340.020 lubdhāḥ krūrāśca mūrkhāśca nivasanti narādhamāḥ (110)|
Vai 340.021 niviṣṭe tūttarāyāṃ ca dhanadhānyasamuccayaḥ |
Vai 340.022 vidyāprakṛtisampanno janaśca kalahapriyaḥ (111)|
Vai 340.023 abhijiti niviṣṭe tu nagare tatra moditāḥ |
Vai 340.024 narāḥ sarve sadā hṛṣṭāḥ parasparānurāgiṇaḥ (112)|
Vai 340.025 śravaṇāyāṃ niviṣṭaṃ tu paraṃ dhānyadhanānvitam |
Vai 340.026 arogijanabhūyiṣṭhasahitaṃ tadvinirdiśet (113)|
Vai 340.027 dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ niviṣṭaṃ tu strījitaṃ puramādiśet |
Vai 340.028 prabhūtavastramālyaṃ ca kāmabhogavivarjitam (114)|
Vai 340.029 pure śatabhiṣāyukte mūrkhaśāṭhyapriyā janāḥ |
Vai 340.030 strīṣu pāneṣu saṃsaktāḥ salilena vinaśyati (115)|
pure proṣṭhapadādhyakṣe narāstatra sukhapriyāḥ |
Vai 341.002 paropatāpino mūrkhā mānakāmavivarjitāḥ (116)|
Vai 341.003 uttarāyāṃ niviṣṭe tu śaśvadvṛddhiranuttarā |
Vai 341.004 pūrṇaṃ ca dhanadhānyābhyāṃ ratnāḍhyaṃ ca vinirdiśet (117)|
Vai 341.005 pure niviṣṭe revatyāṃ sundarī janatā bhavet |
Vai 341.006 kharoṣṭraṃ caiva gāvaśca prabhūtadhanadhānyatā (118)|
Vai 341.007 aśvinyāṃ viniviṣṭaṃ tu nagaraṃ śivamādiśet |
Vai 341.008 arogijanasampūrṇaṃ darśanīyajanākulam (119)|
Vai 341.009 bharaṇyāṃ saṃniviṣṭe tu durbhagāḥ kalahapriyāḥ |
Vai 341.010 duḥśīlā duḥkhabhājaśca vasanti puruṣādhamāḥ (120)|
Vai 341.011 purāṇi rāṣṭrāṇi tathā gṛhāṇi nakṣatrayogaṃ prasamīkṣya vidvān |
Vai 341.013 iṣṭe praśaste ca niveśayettu pūrve ca janme ’dhigataṃ mayedam (121)|
Vai 341.015 ayaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinnakṣatranirdeśo nāmādhyāyaḥ |
|
Vai 341.016 atha khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aṣṭāviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ sthānanirdeśaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ pravakṣyāmi |
Vai 341.017 tacchrūyatām |
kathayatu bhagavān—Vai 341.018 kṛttikā bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatraṃ kaliṅgamagadhānām |
rohiṇī sarvaprajāyāḥ |
Vai 341.019 mṛgaśirā videhānāṃ rājopasevakānāṃ ca |
evamārdrā kṣatriyāṇāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca |
punarvasuḥ sauparṇānām |
Vai 341.020 puṣyanakṣatraṃ sarveṣāmavadātavasanānāṃ rājapadasevakānāṃ ca |
āśleṣā nāgānāṃ haimavatānāṃ ca |
Vai 341.021 maghānakṣatraṃ gauḍikānām |
pūrvaphalgunī caurāṇām |
uttaraphalgunī avantīnām |
Vai 341.022 hastā saurāṣṭrikāṇām |
citrā pakṣiṇāṃ dvipadānām |
svātī sarveṣāṃ pravarajyāsamāpannānām |
Vai 341.023 viśākhā audakānām |
anurādhā vāṇijakānāṃ śākaṭikānāṃ ca |
jyeṣṭhā dauvālikānām |
Vai 341.024 mūlā pathikānām |
pūrvāṣāḍhā bāhlīkānāṃ ca |
uttarāṣāḍhā kāmbojānām |
Vai 341.025 abhijitsarveṣāṃ dakṣiṇāpathikānāṃ tāmraparṇikānāṃ ca |
śravaṇā ghātakānāṃ caurāṇāṃ ca |
dhaniṣṭhā kurupāñcālānām |
Vai 341.026 śatabhiṣā maulikānāmātharvaṇikānāṃ ca |
pūrvabhādrapadā gandhikānām yavanakāmbojānāṃ ca |
Vai 341.027 uttarabhādrapadā gandharvāṇām |
revatī nāvikānāṃ ca |
aśvinī aśvavāṇijānāṃ ca |
Vai 341.028 bharaṇī bhadrapadakarmaṇāṃ bhadrakāyakānāṃ ca |
|
ayaṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatrāṇāṃ sthānanirdeśavyākaraṇo nāmādhyāyaḥ |
|
Vai 341.030 paṭha bhostriśaṅko ṛtuvaṣa nāmādhyāyam |
tadahaṃ vakṣye śrūyatām |
kathayatu bhagavān—kṛttikāsu grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.002 varṣo daśarātrikaḥ |
śravaṇāyuktaproṣṭhapadāyām agrodako varṣārātro bhavati |
Vai 342.003 agnibhayaṃ śastrabhayaṃ codakabhayaṃ ca bhavati |
Vai 342.004 uktaṃ kṛttikāsu |
|
Vai 342.005 rohiṇyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ekaviṃśatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.006 tatra niṃnāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni |
eṣa ca varṣārātraḥ sāroparodhaḥ sasyaṃ ca saṃpādayati |
Vai 342.007 dvau cātra rogau prabalau bhavataḥ |
kukṣirogaścakṣūrogaśca |
caurabahulāścātra diśo bhavanti |
Vai 342.008 uktaṃ ca rohiṇyām |
|
Vai 342.009 mṛgaśīrṣe grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.010 sāroparodho varṣārātraḥ |
paścādvarṣaṃ saṃjanayati |
nikṣiptaśastrāścātra rājāno bhavanti |
kṣemiṇaḥ sunītikāśca diśo bhavanti |
Vai 342.011 muditāścātra janapadā bhavanti |
uktaṃ mṛgaśirasi |
|
Vai 342.012 ārdrāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, aṣṭādaśāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.013 tatra niṃnāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni |
nidhayaśca rakṣayitavyāḥ |
Vai 342.014 caurabahulāścātra diśo bhavanti |
nikṣiptaśastrāśca rajāno bhavanti |
trayaścātra rogāḥ prabalā bhavanti—jvaraḥ śvāso galagrahaśca |
Vai 342.015 bālānāṃ dārakadārikāṇāṃ ca maraṇaṃ bhavati |
ityuktamārdrāyām |
|
Vai 342.016 punarvasau grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, navatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.017 mahāmeghānutpādayati |
āṣāḍhāyāṃ praviṣṭāyāṃ mṛdūni pravarṣati |
anantaraṃ ca nirantareṇa pravarṣati |
Vai 342.018 nikṣiptaśastrāścātra rājāno bhavanti |
uktaṃ punarvasau |
|
Vai 342.019 puṣye grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, dvātriṃśadāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
atra niṃnāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
Vai 342.020 sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni |
vyaktaṃ pradhānavarṣāṇi bhavanti |
sasyaṃ ca niṣpādayati |
Vai 342.021 brāhmaṇakṣatriyāṇāṃ ca virodho bhavati |
daṃṣṭriṇaścātra prabalā bhavanti |
tatra trayo rogāśca bhavanti—gāṇḍāḥ piṭakāḥ pāmāni ca |
Vai 342.022 ityuktaṃ puṣye |
|
Vai 342.023 āśleṣāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ekaviṃśatyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.024 tatra niṃnāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni |
viṣamāśca vāyavo vānti |
Vai 342.025 saṃvignāścātra jñānino rājānaśca bhavanti |
eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni saṃpādayati |
jāyāpatikānāṃ rājāmātyānāṃ ca virodho bhavati |
Vai 342.026 uktamāśleṣāyām |
|
Vai 342.027 maghāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.028 eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni saṃpādayati |
mṛgapakṣipaśumanuṣyāṇāṃ cātra garbhā vinaśyanti |
Vai 342.029 janamaraṇaṃ cātra bhaviṣyatīti |
uktaṃ maghāyām |
|
Vai 342.030 pūrvaphalgunyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 342.031 eṣo varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni saṃpādayati |
tacca sasyaṃ janayitvā paracakrapīḍitā manuṣyā na sukhenopabhuñjate |
Vai 342.032 paśūnāṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ cātra garbhāḥ sukhino bhavanti |
uktaṃ pūrvaphalgunyām |
|
uttaraphalgunyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, aśītyāḍakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.002 eko varṣaḥ sarvasyāni ca saṃpādayati |
nikṣiptaśastrāścātra rājāno bhavanti |
Vai 343.003 brahmakṣatriyayośca virodho bhavati |
kṣipraṃ ca anītikāḥ prajā vinaśyanti |
uktamuttaraphalgunyām |
|
Vai 343.005 haste grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse devaḥ pravarṣati, ekonapañcāśadāḍakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.006 devaśca tadyathā parikṣipti |
patitāni ca sasyārasāgrāṇi anudagrāṇi alpasāraṇyalpodakāni |
Vai 343.007 durbhikṣaścātra bhaviṣyati |
uktaṃ haste |
|
Vai 343.008 citrāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.009 sāroparodhāstataḥ paścādvarṣaṃ saṃjanayati |
nikṣiptaśastrāśca rājāno bhavanti |
muditāścātra janapadā bhavanti |
Vai 343.010 uktaṃ citrāyām |
|
Vai 343.011 svātyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ekaviṃśatyāḍakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.012 nikṣiptaśastrāśca rājāno bhavanti |
caurāścātra balavattarā bhavanti |
uktaṃ svātyām |
|
Vai 343.013 viśākhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, aśītyāḍakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.014 eko varṣaḥ sarvasyāni saṃpādayati |
rājānaścātra cchidrayuktā bhavanti |
agnidāhāścātra prabalā bhavanti |
Vai 343.015 daṃṣṭriṇaścātra balavanto ’pi kṣayaṃ gacchanti |
uktaṃ viśākhāyām |
|
Vai 343.016 anurādhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ṣaṣṭyāḍakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.017 jyeṣṭhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse cātra dṛḍāni bhavanti |
uktamanurādhāyām |
|
Vai 343.018 jyeṣṭhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ṣoḍaśāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.019 tatra kṛṣikarmāntāni pratisaṃhartavyāni |
yugavaratrāṇi varjayitavyāni |
svadhānyāni upasaṃhartavyāni |
Vai 343.020 agnayaḥ pratisaṃhartavyāḥ |
lā.ṅgalāni pratisaṃhartavyāni |
avaśyamanena janapadena vinaṣṭavyaṃ bhavati |
Vai 343.021 paracakrapīḍito bhavati |
uktaṃ jyeṣṭhāyām |
|
Vai 343.022 mūle grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
ekaḥ sasyaṃ saṃpādayati |
caurabahulāścātra diśo bhavanti |
Vai 343.023 trayaścātra vyādhayo balavanto bhavanti—vātagaṇḍaḥ pārśvaśūlamakṣirogaśca |
Vai 343.024 puṣpaphalāni cātra samṛddhāni bhavanti |
nikṣiptaśastrāścātra rājāno bhavanti |
Vai 343.025 uktaṃ mūle |
|
Vai 343.026 pūrvasyāmāṣāḍhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 343.027 dvau cātra grāhau bhavataḥ |
proṣṭhapade vā āśvayujau vā pakṣe |
eko varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni saṃpādayati |
Vai 343.028 dvau cātra rogau prabalau bhavatah—kukṣirogo ’kṣirogaśca |
uktaṃ pūrvāṣāḍhāyām |
|
Vai 343.029 uttarasyāmāṣāḍhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, pūrṇamāḍhakaśataṃ pravarṣati |
Vai 343.030 tatra sthalāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
niṃnāni parivarjayitavyāni |
mahāsrotāṃsi cātra pravahanti |
Vai 343.031 agrodakā cātra bhavanti |
sarvasasyāni niṣpādayati |
trayaścātra rogāḥ prabalā bhavanti—gaṇḍaḥ kacchaḥ kaṇṭharoga iti |
Vai 343.032 uktamuttarāṣāḍhāyām |
|
abhijiti grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakani pravarṣati |
Vai 344.002 maṇḍalavarṣaṃ ca devaḥ pravarṣati |
paścād varṣaḥ sasyaṃ janayati |
audakānāṃ bhūtānāmutsargo bhavati |
Vai 344.003 uktamabhijiti |
|
Vai 344.004 śravaṇe tu grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 344.005 maṇḍalavarṣaṃ ca devo varṣati |
paścād varṣā sasyaṃ saṃpādayati |
audakānāṃ bhūtānāmutsargo bhavati |
Vai 344.006 vyādhibahulāśca narā bhavanti |
rājānaśca tīvradaṇḍā bhavanti |
uktaṃ śravaṇe |
|
Vai 344.007 dhaniṣṭhāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, ekapañcādāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 344.008 vibhaktāścātra varṣā bhavanti |
tatra niṃnāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni |
Vai 344.009 durmukho rātrau varṣo bhavati |
sasyāni saṃpādayati |
ekaścātra rogo bhavati—gaṇḍavikāraḥ |
Vai 344.010 śastrasamādānāśca rājāno bhavanti |
uktaṃ dhaniṣṭhāyām |
|
Vai 344.011 śatabhiṣāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra pravarṣati, ṣoḍaśāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 344.012 tatra niṃnāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
sthalāni parivarjayitavyāni |
eko varṣaḥ sarvasasyāni saṃpādayati |
Vai 344.013 cakrasamārūḍhā janapadā bhavanti |
manuṣyā dārakadārikāśca skandhe kṛtvā deśāntaraṃ gacchanti |
Vai 344.014 uktaṃ śatabhiṣāyām |
|
Vai 344.015 pūrvasyāṃ bhādrapadāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime māse yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, catuḥṣaṣṭyāḍhakāni pravarṣati |
Vai 344.016 varṣāmukhe cātra ekonaviṃśatirātriko ’vagraho bhavati |
puṣpasasyaṃ ca nāśayati |
Vai 344.017 etāścād varṣā bahucaurā bhavanti |
dvau cātra mahāvyādhī bhavatah—prathamaṃ pittatāpajvaro bhavati, paścād balavān mahāgraho bhavati |
Vai 344.018 martyānāṃ nārīṇāṃ ca maraṇaṃ bhavati |
Vai 344.019 uktaṃ pūrvabhādrapadāyām |
|
Vai 344.020 uttarasyāṃ bhādrapadāyāṃ grīṣmāṇāṃ paścime yadyatra devaḥ pravarṣati, pūrṇamāḍhakaśataṃ pravarṣati |
Vai 344.021 mahāsrotāṃsi pravahanti |
grāmanagaranigamāḥ srotasā uhyante |
catvāraścātra vyādhayaḥ prabalā bhavanti |
Vai 344.022 tadyathā—kukṣirogo ’kṣirogaḥ kāso jvaraśceti |
bālānāṃ dārakadārikāṇāṃ maraṇaṃ bhavati |
Vai 344.023 atra sthalāni kṛṣikartavyāni |
niṃnāni parivarjayitavyāni |
Vai 344.024 etāśca varṣāḥ puṣpāṇi phalāni ca saṃpādayanti |
uktamuttarabhādrapadāyām |
|

Vai 345.006 amīṣāṃ bhoḥ puṣkarasārinn aṣṭāviṃśatīnāṃ nakṣatrāṇāṃ rāhugrahe phalavipākaṃ vyākhyāsyāmi |
Vai 345.007 kṛttikāsu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin yadi candragraho bhavati, kaliṅgamagadhānāmupapīḍā bhavati |
Vai 345.008 yadi rohiṇyāṃ candragraho bhavati, prajānāmupapīḍā bhavati |

Vai 345.015 yadi viśākhāyāṃ somo gṛhyate, audakānāṃ sattvānāmupapīḍā bhavati |
Vai 345.016 yadyanurādhāsu somo gṛhyate, vaṇijānāmupapīḍā bhavati śākaṭikānāṃ ca |

Vai 353.024 evamabhinirdiṣṭaṃ vā svasti kṣipraṃ bhaviṣyati (228)|

Vai 354.005 pañca khalu bhoḥ puṣkarasārin nakṣatrāṇi dāruṇāni bhavanti |
tadyathā—Vai 354.006 maghā trīṇi ca pūrvāṇi bharaṇī ceti pañcamī |
Vai 354.007 athātra dagdhaṃ naṣṭaṃ vā viddhaṃ vā na bhaviṣyati (232)|
Vai 354.008 iti vaktavyam |
ardharātrikāṇi ṣaṭ |
tadyathā—ārdrā āśleṣā svātī jyeṣṭhā śatabhiṣā bharaṇī ceti |
Vai 354.009 navāṃśāḥ ṣaḍgrāsā dvikṣetrāṇi |
rohiṇī punarvasurviśākhā ca |
Vai 354.010 trīṇi uttarāṇi ceti ubhayatovibhāgāni |
pañcadaśa kṣetrāṇi |
kṛttikā ca maghā mūlā trīṇi pūrvāṇi |
Vai 354.011 imāni ṣaṭ pūrvabhāgikāni |
mṛgaśirā puṣyā hastā citrā anurādhā śravaṇā dhaniṣṭhā revatī aśvinī ceti imāni nava nakṣatrāṇi pañcādbhāgīyāni triṃśanmuhūrtayogāni kṣetrāṇi ca |

Vai 354.014 api ca brāhmaṇa śubhāśca muhūrtā bhavanti, aśubhāśca muhūrtā bhavanti, śubhāśubhāśca muhūrtā bhavanti |
Vai 354.015 saṃprayuktanakṣatreṣu sarveṣu yadā śubhamuhūrtasamāpattayo bhavanti, tadā śobhanā bhavanti |
Vai 354.016 yadā aśubhamuhūrtasamāpattayo bhavanti, tadā na śobhanā bhavanti |
yadā tu punaḥ śubhāścāśubhāśca samāpattayo, tadā sādhāraṇā bhavanti |
|
Vai 354.018 athātra kathaṃ rātridivasānāṃ hrāso vṛddhirvā bhavatīti taducyate |
varṣāṇāṃ prathame māse puṣyanakṣatramamāvāsyāṃ bhavati, śravaṇā pūrṇamāsyām |
Vai 354.019 aṣṭādaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |
Vai 354.020 dvādaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ |
ṣoḍaśāṅgulakāṣṭhasya madhyāhne ’rdhāṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyāmādityaḥ parivartate |
Vai 354.021 āṣāḍhā rātriṃ nayati |
mṛgaśirasi ādityo gato bhavati |
varṣāṇāṃ dvitīye māse maghā amāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati, bhādrapadā pūrṇamāsyām |
Vai 354.022 saptadaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |
trayodaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ |
Vai 354.023 dvyaṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyāmādityaḥ parivartate |
śravaṇā rātriṃ nayati |
puṣya ādityo gato bhavati |
Vai 354.024 varṣāṇāṃ tṛtīye māse phalgunyamāvāsyāyāṃ bhavati, aśvinī pūrṇamāsyām |
Vai 354.025 ṣoḍaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |
caturdaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ |
cauraṅgulāyāṃ chāyāyāmādityaḥ parivartate |
Vai 354.026 pūrvabhādrapadā rātriṃ nayati |
Vai 354.027 maghāyāmādityo gato bhavati |

pañcadaśamuhūrto bhavati divasaḥ |
pañcadaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ |

caturdaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |

Vai 355.001 citrāyāmādityo gato bhavati |

Vai 355.002 trayodaśamuhūrto divaso bhavati |
saptadaśamuhūrtā rātriḥ |
